class FeatureBuilder(_object):
    """
    @brief A base class for all Builders.
    @details
     A Builder is an object that is used to create and edit Features.

     This is an abstract class that provides the basic functionality common to all builders. See the Builder subclasses for details of application-specific builders.

     This is an abstract class, and cannot be instantiated.
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, FeatureBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, FeatureBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_FeatureBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def Commit(self):
        """
        @brief Commits any edits that have been applied to the builder.
        @details
         Commits any edits that have been applied to the feature being edited, or a new feature if the builder is being used in creation mode.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureBuilder_Commit(self)


    def ShowResult(self):
        """@brief Updates the feature to reflect the result of an edit to the feature for all builders that support showing results."""
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureBuilder_ShowResult(self)


    def __GetFeature(self):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureBuilder___GetFeature(self)

    def __GetStatus(self):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureBuilder___GetStatus(self)

    def __GetName(self):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureBuilder___GetName(self)

    def __SetName(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureBuilder___SetName(self, value)

    def __GetFullName(self):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureBuilder___GetFullName(self)

    def __GetNameWithContext(self):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureBuilder___GetNameWithContext(self)

    
    Feature = property(fget = __GetFeature)
    
    FullName = property(fget = __GetFullName)
    
    Name = property(fget = __GetName, fset = __SetName)
    
    NameWithContext = property(fget = __GetNameWithContext)
    
    Status = property(fget = __GetStatus)

FeatureBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.FeatureBuilder_swigregister
FeatureBuilder_swigregister(FeatureBuilder)

class OpticalPropertiesGeometry(_object):
    """
    @brief Represents interface for editing optical properties geometries.
    @details
     This interface is used to edit geometries on which the optical properties are applied.


     To create a new instance of this class, use @link COpticalPropertiesBuilder::GetOpticalPropertiesGeometry @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, OpticalPropertiesGeometry, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, OpticalPropertiesGeometry, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_OpticalPropertiesGeometry
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def Add(self, tag):
        """
        @brief Adds a geometry.
        @details
         The Add function takes a geometry tag.
        @param[in] tag: Integer.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesGeometry_Add(self, tag)


    def Remove(self, tag):
        """
        @brief Removes a feature.
        @details
         The Remove function takes a geometry tag.
        @param[in] tag: Integer.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesGeometry_Remove(self, tag)


    def Clear(self):
        """@brief Clear all geometries."""
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesGeometry_Clear(self)


    def SetDirection(self, tag, value):
        """
        @brief Sets a direction for a certain geometry.
        @details
         The SetDirection function takes a feature tag as the first parameter.<br>
         The function changes the direction of a geometry.<br>

         The reverse direction depends of the value parameter:<br>
         0 - Does not reverse the direction.<br>
         1 - Reverses the direction.
        @param[in] tag : Integer.
        @param[in] value : Integer.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesGeometry_SetDirection(self, tag, value)


    def RevertGeometry(self, tag):
        """
        @brief Reverts a geometry.
        @details
         The RevertFace function takes a feature tag.
        @param[in] tag : Integer.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesGeometry_RevertGeometry(self, tag)


    def __SetGeometryList(self, tags):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesGeometry___SetGeometryList(self, tags)

    def __GetGeometryList(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesGeometry___GetGeometryList(self)

    
    GeometryList = property(fget = __GetGeometryList, fset = __SetGeometryList)

OpticalPropertiesGeometry_swigregister = _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesGeometry_swigregister
OpticalPropertiesGeometry_swigregister(OpticalPropertiesGeometry)

class FeatureCollection(_object):
    """
    @brief Represents the collection of Speos features in a Part.
    @details
     There is only one instance of FeatureCollection for each Part.<br>
     To obtain an instance of this class, refer to Part.<br>
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, FeatureCollection, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, FeatureCollection, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_FeatureCollection
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def FindFromTag(self, tag):
        """
        @brief Finds the feature with the given Tag.
        @details 
         This function takes as parameter a feature tag.
        @param[in] Tag : Integer.
        @return The feature with the given Tag.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_FindFromTag(self, tag)


    def FindFromName(self, name):
        """
        @brief Finds the feature with the given name.
        @details 
         This function only accepts full a feature name (e.g., "Direct Simulation (0)").<br>
        @param[in] name : String.
        @return The feature with the given name.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_FindFromName(self, name)


    def __GetSourceFeatures(self):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection___GetSourceFeatures(self)

    def __GetSensorFeatures(self):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection___GetSensorFeatures(self)

    def __GetOpticalPropertyFeatures(self):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection___GetOpticalPropertyFeatures(self)

    def __GetSimulationFeatures(self):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection___GetSimulationFeatures(self)

    def CreateSourceDisplayBuilder(self, featureToEdit):
        """
        @brief Creates a builder for a display source.
        @param[in] featureToEdit: the feature to be edited or None to create a new feature.
        @return SourceDisplayBuilder object.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_CreateSourceDisplayBuilder(self, featureToEdit)


    def CreateSourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder(self, featureToEdit):
        """
        @brief Creates a builder for an ambient source with CIE General Sky type.
        @param[in] featureToEdit: the feature to be edited or None to create a new feature.
        @return SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder object.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_CreateSourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder(self, featureToEdit)


    def CreateSourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder(self, featureToEdit):
        """
        @brief Creates a builder for an ambient source with Natural Light type.
        @param[in] featureToEdit: the feature to be edited or None to create a new feature.
        @return SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder object.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_CreateSourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder(self, featureToEdit)


    def CreateSourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder(self, featureToEdit):
        """
        @brief Creates a builder for an ambient source with Overcast Sky type.
        @param[in] featureToEdit: the feature to be edited or None to create a new feature.
        @return SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder object.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_CreateSourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder(self, featureToEdit)


    def CreateSourceAmbientUniformBuilder(self, featureToEdit):
        """
        @brief Creates a builder for an ambient source with Uniform type.
        @param[in] featureToEdit: the feature to be edited or None to create a new feature.
        @return SourceAmbientUniformBuilder object.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_CreateSourceAmbientUniformBuilder(self, featureToEdit)


    def CreateSourceAmbientUS1976Builder(self, featureToEdit):
        """
        @brief Creates a builder for an U.S. Standard Atmosphere 1976 source.

        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_CreateSourceAmbientUS1976Builder(self, featureToEdit)


    def CreateSourceLuminaireBuilder(self, featureToEdit):
        """
        @brief Creates a builder for a luminaire source.

        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_CreateSourceLuminaireBuilder(self, featureToEdit)


    def CreateSourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder(self, featureToEdit):
        """
        @brief Creates a builder for an ambient environment source.
        @param[in] featureToEdit: the feature to be edited or None to create a new feature.
        @return SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder object.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_CreateSourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder(self, featureToEdit)


    def CreateSourceSurfaceBuilder(self, featureToEdit):
        """
        @brief Creates a builder for a surface source.
        @param[in] featureToEdit: the feature to be edited or None to create a new feature.
        @return SourceSurfaceBuilder object.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_CreateSourceSurfaceBuilder(self, featureToEdit)


    def CreateSourceRayFileBuilder(self, featureToEdit):
        """
        @brief Creates a builder for a ray file source.

        @return SourceRayFileBuilder object.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureCollection_CreateSourceRayFileBuilder(self, featureToEdit)


    def CreateSensorRadianceBuilder(self, featureToEdit):
        """

class AxisSystem(_object):
    """
    @brief Represents an Axis System.
    @details 
     This object is composed of an origin point, X and Y directions.<br>

     This class cannot be instantiated.<br>
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, AxisSystem, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, AxisSystem, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __SetOriginPoint(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.AxisSystem___SetOriginPoint(self, tag)

    def __GetOriginPoint(self):
        return _SpeosNX.AxisSystem___GetOriginPoint(self)

    def __SetDirectionX(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.AxisSystem___SetDirectionX(self, tag)

    def __GetDirectionX(self):
        return _SpeosNX.AxisSystem___GetDirectionX(self)

    def __SetDirectionXReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.AxisSystem___SetDirectionXReversed(self, value)

    def __GetDirectionXReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.AxisSystem___GetDirectionXReversed(self)

    def __SetDirectionY(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.AxisSystem___SetDirectionY(self, tag)

    def __GetDirectionY(self):
        return _SpeosNX.AxisSystem___GetDirectionY(self)

    def __SetDirectionYReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.AxisSystem___SetDirectionYReversed(self, value)

    def __GetDirectionYReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.AxisSystem___GetDirectionYReversed(self)

    
    DirectionX = property(fget = __GetDirectionX, fset = __SetDirectionX)
    
    DirectionXReversed = property(fget = __GetDirectionXReversed, fset = __SetDirectionXReversed)
    
    DirectionY = property(fget = __GetDirectionY, fset = __SetDirectionY)
    
    DirectionYReversed = property(fget = __GetDirectionYReversed, fset = __SetDirectionYReversed)
    
    OriginPoint = property(fget = __GetOriginPoint, fset = __SetOriginPoint)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_AxisSystem
    __del__ = lambda self: None
AxisSystem_swigregister = _SpeosNX.AxisSystem_swigregister
AxisSystem_swigregister(AxisSystem)

class Preset(_object):
    """
    @brief Represents a Preset.
    @details 
     This class cannot be instantiated.<br>
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, Preset, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, Preset, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_Preset
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def __GetName(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Preset___GetName(self)

    def Rename(self, value):
        """
        @brief Renames the preset.
        @param[in] value : String
        """
        return _SpeosNX.Preset_Rename(self, value)


    def Delete(self):
        """@brief Deletes the preset."""
        return _SpeosNX.Preset_Delete(self)

    __swig_setmethods__["m_pImpl"] = _SpeosNX.Preset_m_pImpl_set
    __swig_getmethods__["m_pImpl"] = _SpeosNX.Preset_m_pImpl_get
    if _newclass:
        m_pImpl = _swig_property(_SpeosNX.Preset_m_pImpl_get, _SpeosNX.Preset_m_pImpl_set)

    
    Name = property(fget = __GetName)

Preset_swigregister = _SpeosNX.Preset_swigregister
Preset_swigregister(Preset)

class SensorFilter(_object):
    """@brief Data Model for Sensor Filter"""

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SensorFilter, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SensorFilter, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetLayerType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___GetLayerType(self)

    def __SetLayerType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___SetLayerType(self, value)

    def __GetSurfaceContributionType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___GetSurfaceContributionType(self)

    def __SetSurfaceContributionType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___SetSurfaceContributionType(self, value)

    def __GetSurfaceContribution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___GetSurfaceContribution(self)

    def __SetSurfaceContribution(self, faces):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___SetSurfaceContribution(self, faces)

    def __GetSurfaceContributionNumber(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___GetSurfaceContributionNumber(self)

    def __GetMaximumSequences(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___GetMaximumSequences(self)

    def __SetMaximumSequences(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___SetMaximumSequences(self, value)

    def __GetSequencePerType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___GetSequencePerType(self)

    def __SetSequencePerType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___SetSequencePerType(self, value)

    def __GetSortSequencePerType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___GetSortSequencePerType(self)

    def __SetSortSequencePerType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorFilter___SetSortSequencePerType(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the type of filter.
    # @details 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - None. Get the simulation's results in one layer.<br>
    #  1 - Data Separated by Source. <br>
    #  2 - Data Separated by Face. <br>
    #  3 - Data Separated by Sequence.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    LayerType = property(fget = __GetLayerType, fset = __SetLayerType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the maximum number of sequences.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The Type property must be 3.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 10.
    MaximumSequences = property(fget = __GetMaximumSequences, fset = __SetMaximumSequences)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the sequence per type.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The Type property must be 3.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Faces.<br>
    #  1 - Volumes.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    SequencePerType = property(fget = __GetSequencePerType, fset = __SetSequencePerType)
    SortSequencePerType = property(fget = __GetSortSequencePerType, fset = __SetSortSequencePerType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the surface contribution.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The Type property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  The SurfaceContribution property takes a list of feature tags and returns a list of feature tags. 
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty list.
    SurfaceContribution = property(fget = __GetSurfaceContribution, fset = __SetSurfaceContribution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the surface contribution number.
    # @details 
    #  Returns the number of the selected surface contribution.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.
    SurfaceContributionNumber = property(fget = __GetSurfaceContributionNumber)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the surface contribution type.
    # @details 
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The Type property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are: <br>
    #  0 - The Last impact.<br>
    #  1 - Intersected One Time.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    SurfaceContributionType = property(fget = __GetSurfaceContributionType, fset = __SetSurfaceContributionType)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SensorFilter
    __del__ = lambda self: None
SensorFilter_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SensorFilter_swigregister
SensorFilter_swigregister(SensorFilter)

        return _SpeosNX.SimulationSettings___SetTextureNormalizationMode(self, value)

    def __GetRenderingAsOptical(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationSettings___GetRenderingAsOptical(self)

    def __SetRenderingAsOptical(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationSettings___SetRenderingAsOptical(self, value)

    def SaveAsPreset(self, name):
        """
        @brief Save the simulation settings as preset.
        @param[in] name :  name of the preset.
        @return
         True: Success.<br>
         False: Error.<br>
        """
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationSettings_SaveAsPreset(self, name)

    __swig_setmethods__["m_pImpl"] = _SpeosNX.SimulationSettings_m_pImpl_set
    __swig_getmethods__["m_pImpl"] = _SpeosNX.SimulationSettings_m_pImpl_get
    if _newclass:
        m_pImpl = _swig_property(_SpeosNX.SimulationSettings_m_pImpl_get, _SpeosNX.SimulationSettings_m_pImpl_set)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ambient sampling.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be False.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [1, 1000000].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    AmbientSampling = property(fget = __GetAmbientSampling, fset = __SetAmbientSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the anti-aliasing property.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be False.<br>
    #  True: Uses anti-aliasing.<br>
    #  False: Does not use anti-aliasing.<br>
    # 
    #  Reduces artifacts as jagged profiles and fine details but increasing the simulation time.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    AntiAliasing = property(fget = __GetAntiAliasing, fset = __SetAntiAliasing)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the colorimetric standard type.
    # @details
    #  The values are: <br>
    #  0 - CIE 1931.<br>
    #  1 - CIE 1936.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ColorimetricStandardMode = property(fget = __GetColorimetricStandardMode, fset = __SetColorimetricStandardMode)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the specular approximation angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The PhotonMapMode property must be 1 or 3.<br>
    #  
    #  Represents the max impact of rays in the direct phase.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    DirectMaxImpact = property(fget = __GetDirectMaxImpact, fset = __SetDirectMaxImpact)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the specular approximation angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The PhotonMapMode property must be 1 or 3.<br>
    #  
    #  Represents the number of rays sent in the direct phase.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: (0, 200000].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 10000.
    DirectPhotonNumber = property(fget = __GetDirectPhotonNumber, fset = __SetDirectPhotonNumber)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to use dispersion.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be True.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Activates dispersion.<br>
    #  False: Deactivates dispersion.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    Dispersion = property(fget = __GetDispersion, fset = __SetDispersion)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to draw impacts.
    # @details
    #  Displays the impacts in the 3D view.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Draws impacts.<br>
    #  False: Does not draw impacts.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    DrawImpacts = property(fget = __GetDrawImpacts, fset = __SetDrawImpacts)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to draw rays.
    # @details
    #  Displays the ray trajectories in the 3D view.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Draws rays.<br>
    #  False: Does not draw rays.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    DrawRays = property(fget = __GetDrawRays, fset = __SetDrawRays)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the fast transmission gathering property.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be True.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Uses fast transmission gathering.<br>
    #  False: Does not use fast transmission gathering.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    FastTransmissionGathering = property(fget = __GetFastTransmissionGathering, fset = __SetFastTransmissionGathering)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the final gathering property.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The PhotonMapMode property must be 1, 2 or 3.<br>
    #  True: Uses final gathering.<br>
    #  False: Does not use final gathering.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    FinalGathering = property(fget = __GetFinalGathering, fset = __SetFinalGathering)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the final gathering neighbors.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseFinalGathering property must be True.<br>
    # 
    #  Pilots the number of neighbors after the secondary rays. They are used to compute the luminance for each split ray.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 10.
    FinalGatheringNeighbors = property(fget = __GetFinalGatheringNeighbors, fset = __SetFinalGatheringNeighbors)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the gathering source number.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  The gathering source number parameter pilots the number of shadow rays to target at each source.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 1.
    GatheringSourceNumber = property(fget = __GetGatheringSourceNumber, fset = __SetGatheringSourceNumber)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the geometrical distance tolerance.
    # @details
    #  The Geometrical distance tolerance defines the maximum distance to consider two faces as tangent.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.05 mm.
    GeometricalDistanceTolerance = property(fget = __GetGeometricalDistanceTolerance, fset = __SetGeometricalDistanceTolerance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to report impact.
    # @details
    #  Activates the addition of information to the HTML simulation report.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Reports impacts.<br>
    #  False: Does not report impacts.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    InteractiveSimulationReport = property(fget = __GetInteractiveSimulationReport, fset = __SetInteractiveSimulationReport)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the intermediate save frequency.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer (in seconds).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 300.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 1800 s.
    IntermediateSaveFrequency = property(fget = __GetIntermediateSaveFrequency, fset = __SetIntermediateSaveFrequency)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the maximum gathering error.
    # @details
    #   <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  Defines the level below which a source can be neglected.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0.0, 100.0].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.0.
    MaxGatheringError = property(fget = __GetMaxGatheringError, fset = __SetMaxGatheringError)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the maximum neighbors.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The PhotonMapMode property must be 1, 2 or 3.<br>
    #  
    #  Represents the number of photons from the photon map taken into account to calculate the luminance.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: (0, 10000].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    MaxNeighbors = property(fget = __GetMaxNeighbors, fset = __SetMaxNeighbors)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the maximum search radius.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The PhotonMapMode property must be 1, 2 or 3.<br>
    #  
    #  Represents the maximum distance from the luminance calculation's point to search for neighbors contribution.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>:The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100000000.0 mm.
    MaxSearchRadius = property(fget = __GetMaxSearchRadius, fset = __SetMaxSearchRadius)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the maximum number of surface interaction.
    # @details
    #  The maximum number of surface interactions value defines the maximum number of ray impacts during propagation. <br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    MaximumImpactNumber = property(fget = __GetMaximumImpactNumber, fset = __SetMaximumImpactNumber)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: (0.0, 90.0).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 15.0 degrees.
    MeshingAngle = property(fget = __GetMeshingAngle, fset = __SetMeshingAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing edge angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b> The UseSpecificFacetEdgesParam property must be True.
    #  
    #  Defines the maximum angular variation in degrees between successive tangents for all points along a solid edge.
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: (0.0, 90.0).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 10.0 degrees.
    MeshingEdgeAngle = property(fget = __GetMeshingEdgeAngle, fset = __SetMeshingEdgeAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing edge sag value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b> The UseSpecificFacetEdgesParam property must be True.
    #  
    #  Defines the maximum distance between the geometry and the meshing on the edges. The Meshing edge sag value always uses the Fixed mode.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.1 mm.
    MeshingEdgeSag = property(fget = __GetMeshingEdgeSag, fset = __SetMeshingEdgeSag)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing sag mode.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Proportional, the value adapts and adjusts to the size of each face of the object. <br>
    #  1 - Fixed, the value will remain unchanged no matter the size or shape of the object. <br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    MeshingSagMode = property(fget = __GetMeshingSagMode, fset = __SetMeshingSagMode)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing sag value.
    # @details
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.5 mm.
    MeshingSagValue = property(fget = __GetMeshingSagValue, fset = __SetMeshingSagValue)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing step mode.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Proportional, the value adapts and adjusts to the size of each face of the object.<br>
    #  1 - Fixed, the value will remain unchanged no matter the size or shape of the object.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    MeshingStepMode = property(fget = __GetMeshingStepMode, fset = __SetMeshingStepMode)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing step fixed value.
    # @details
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 1.0 mm.
    MeshingStepValue = property(fget = __GetMeshingStepValue, fset = __SetMeshingStepValue)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the maximum number of surface interaction.
    # @details
    #  
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b> The UseWeight property must be True.<br>
    # 
    #  The Minimum energy percentage value defines the minimum energy ratio to continue to propagate a ray with weight. <br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0.0, 10000.0]<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.5.
    MinimumEnergy = property(fget = __GetMinimumEnergy, fset = __SetMinimumEnergy)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Monte Carlo algorithm property.
    # @details
    #  True: Uses Monte Carlo algorithm.<br>
    #  False: Uses deterministic algorithm.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    MonteCarloAlgorithm = property(fget = __GetMonteCarloAlgorithm, fset = __SetMonteCarloAlgorithm)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the number of standard passes before optimized passes.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The OptimizedMode property must be 1 or 2.<br>
    # 
    #  Corresponds to the minimum number of passes without pass optimization.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    NumberStandardPasses = property(fget = __GetNumberStandardPasses, fset = __SetNumberStandardPasses)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets optimized propagation type.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - None, the same number of passes is used for each pixel of the image.<br>
    #  1 - Relative, the algorithm adapts the number of passes per pixel to send the optimal number of rays according to the signal each pixel needs.<br>
    #  2 - Absolute, same as relative, however the method of calculation is slightly different.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    OptimizedPropagation = property(fget = __GetOptimizedPropagation, fset = __SetOptimizedPropagation)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the photon map mode.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be False.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - No photon map.<br>
    #  1 - Build photon map.<br>
    #  2 - Load photon map.<br>
    #  3 - Build and save photon map.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    PhotonMapMode = property(fget = __GetPhotonMapMode, fset = __SetPhotonMapMode)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets ray tracer precision mode.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Automatic.<br>
    #  1 - Double.<br>
    #  2 - Single.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    RayTracerPrecisionMode = property(fget = __GetRayTracerPrecisionMode, fset = __SetRayTracerPrecisionMode)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to use rendering as optical properties.
    # @details
    #  True: Uses rendering as optical properties.<br>
    #  False: Does not use rendering as optical properties.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    RenderingAsOptical = property(fget = __GetRenderingAsOptical, fset = __SetRenderingAsOptical)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the intermediate save frequency.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 300.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 1800.
    SaveIntermediateMaps = property(fget = __GetSaveIntermediateMaps, fset = __SetSaveIntermediateMaps)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the smart engine value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The RayTracerPrecisionMode property must be 1.<br>
    # 
    #  The Smart Engine value defines a balance between the speed and the memory. The higher the value, the more subdivided the scene becomes.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [1, 15].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 11.
    SmartEngine = property(fget = __GetSmartEngine, fset = __SetSmartEngine)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the specific parameters property for facet edges.
    # @details
    #  Allows to control the precision of the meshing on the edges of the faces.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Enables specific parameters for facet edges.<br>
    #  False: Disables specific parameters for facet edges.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    SpecificFacetEdgesParameters = property(fget = __GetSpecificFacetEdgesParameters, fset = __SetSpecificFacetEdgesParameters)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the specular approximation angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be False.<br>
    #  
    #  Reduces artifacts as jagged profiles and fine details but increasing the simulation time.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 0.0.
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.0 degrees.
    SpecularApproxAngle = property(fget = __GetSpecularApproxAngle, fset = __SetSpecularApproxAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the specular maximum impact number.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be False.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0, 15].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 10.
    SpecularMaxImpact = property(fget = __GetSpecularMaxImpact, fset = __SetSpecularMaxImpact)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to use splitting for inverse simulation.
    # @details
    #   <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseMonteCarlo property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  If you do so, the path of each reverse propagated ray is split in more paths at the first impact after leaving the observer point.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Activates splitting.<br>
    #  False: Deactivates splitting.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    Splitting = property(fget = __GetSplitting, fset = __SetSplitting)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the splitting number.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseFinalGathering property must be True.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 15.
    SplittingNumber = property(fget = __GetSplittingNumber, fset = __SetSplittingNumber)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to use texture mapping.
    # @details
    #  True: Uses texture as optical properties.<br>
    #  False: Does not use texture as optical properties.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    Texture = property(fget = __GetTexture, fset = __SetTexture)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets texture normalization mode.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseTexture property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are: <br>
    #  0 - None. The simulation results uses both the Image Texture and the Texture Mapping Optical Properties.<br>
    #  1 - Color from BRDF. The simulation result uses the BRDF information of the Texture Mapping Optical Properties.<br>
    #  2 - Color from texture. The simulation result uses the color and the color lightness of the Image Texture.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    TextureNormalizationMode = property(fget = __GetTextureNormalizationMode, fset = __SetTextureNormalizationMode)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the weight property.
    # @details
    #  True: Uses weight.<br>
    #  False: Does not use weight.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    Weight = property(fget = __GetWeight, fset = __SetWeight)

SimulationSettings_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SimulationSettings_swigregister
SimulationSettings_swigregister(SimulationSettings)

class Timezone(_object):
    """
    @brief Represents a Timezone.
    @details 
     This class cannot be instantiated.<br>
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, Timezone, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, Timezone, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetUserDefinedLocation(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetUserDefinedLocation(self)

    def __SetUserDefinedLocation(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetUserDefinedLocation(self, value)

    def __GetLocation(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetLocation(self)

    def __SetLocation(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetLocation(self, value)

    def __GetTimezoneId(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetTimezoneId(self)

    def __SetTimezoneId(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetTimezoneId(self, value)

    def __GetLongitudeDegrees(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetLongitudeDegrees(self)

    def __SetLongitudeDegrees(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetLongitudeDegrees(self, value)

    def __GetLongitudeMinutes(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetLongitudeMinutes(self)

    def __SetLongitudeMinutes(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetLongitudeMinutes(self, value)

    def __GetLongitudeSeconds(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetLongitudeSeconds(self)

    def __SetLongitudeSeconds(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetLongitudeSeconds(self, value)

    def __GetLatitudeDegrees(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetLatitudeDegrees(self)

    def __SetLatitudeDegrees(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetLatitudeDegrees(self, value)

    def __GetLatitudeMinutes(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetLatitudeMinutes(self)

    def __SetLatitudeMinutes(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetLatitudeMinutes(self, value)

    def __GetLatitudeSeconds(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetLatitudeSeconds(self)

    def __SetLatitudeSeconds(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetLatitudeSeconds(self, value)

    def __GetYear(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetYear(self)

    def __SetYear(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetYear(self, value)

    def __GetMonth(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetMonth(self)

    def __SetMonth(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetMonth(self, value)

    def __GetDay(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetDay(self)

    def __SetDay(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetDay(self, value)

    def __GetHour(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetHour(self)

    def __SetHour(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetHour(self, value)

    def __GetMinute(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___GetMinute(self)

    def __SetMinute(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Timezone___SetMinute(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the day.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [1, 31] (in day).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is the current day.
    Day = property(fget = __GetDay, fset = __SetDay)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the hour.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0, 24] (in hour).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is the current hour.
    Hour = property(fget = __GetHour, fset = __SetHour)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the latitude degrees.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The UserDefinedLocation property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer (in degrees).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 43 degrees.
    LatitudeDegrees = property(fget = __GetLatitudeDegrees, fset = __SetLatitudeDegrees)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the latitude minutes.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The UserDefinedLocation property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer (in minute).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 9 minutes.
    LatitudeMinutes = property(fget = __GetLatitudeMinutes, fset = __SetLatitudeMinutes)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the latitude seconds.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The UserDefinedLocation property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer (in second).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 12 seconds.
    LatitudeSeconds = property(fget = __GetLatitudeSeconds, fset = __SetLatitudeSeconds)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets a predefined location.
    # @details 
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The UserDefinedLocation property must be False.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is "ANSYS, France".
    Location = property(fget = __GetLocation, fset = __SetLocation)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the longitude degrees.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The UserDefinedLocation property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer (in degrees).<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 6 degrees.
    LongitudeDegrees = property(fget = __GetLongitudeDegrees, fset = __SetLongitudeDegrees)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the longitude minutes.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The UserDefinedLocation property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer (in minute).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 2 minutes.
    LongitudeMinutes = property(fget = __GetLongitudeMinutes, fset = __SetLongitudeMinutes)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the longitude seconds.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The UserDefinedLocation property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer (in second).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 56 seconds.
    LongitudeSeconds = property(fget = __GetLongitudeSeconds, fset = __SetLongitudeSeconds)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the minute.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0, 59] (in minute).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is the current minute.
    Minute = property(fget = __GetMinute, fset = __SetMinute)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the month.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [1, 12] (in month).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is the current month.
    Month = property(fget = __GetMonth, fset = __SetMonth)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets a timezone by Id.
    # @details
    #  The property UserDefinedLocation must be True.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is "CET".
    TimezoneId = property(fget = __GetTimezoneId, fset = __SetTimezoneId)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable/disable the user defined location.
    # @details
    #  True: Sets the timezone, the Earth coordinates date and time manually.<br>
    #  False: Uses predefined location.
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    UserDefinedLocation = property(fget = __GetUserDefinedLocation, fset = __SetUserDefinedLocation)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the year.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer (in year).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is the current Year.
    Year = property(fget = __GetYear, fset = __SetYear)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_Timezone
    __del__ = lambda self: None
Timezone_swigregister = _SpeosNX.Timezone_swigregister
Timezone_swigregister(Timezone)

class ZenithNorthSystem(_object):
    """
    @brief Represents an Axis System.
    @details
     This object is composed of Zenith and North directions.<br>

     This class cannot be instantiated.<br>
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, ZenithNorthSystem, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, ZenithNorthSystem, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetZenithDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.ZenithNorthSystem___GetZenithDirection(self)

    def __SetZenithDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.ZenithNorthSystem___SetZenithDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetZenithDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.ZenithNorthSystem___GetZenithDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetZenithDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.ZenithNorthSystem___SetZenithDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetNorthDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.ZenithNorthSystem___GetNorthDirection(self)

    def __SetNorthDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.ZenithNorthSystem___SetNorthDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetNorthDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.ZenithNorthSystem___GetNorthDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetNorthDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.ZenithNorthSystem___SetNorthDirectionReversed(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the north direction.
    # @details
    #  The North direction property takes and returns a Tag from an NX object.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    NorthDirection = property(fget = __GetNorthDirection, fset = __SetNorthDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reverse North direction.
    # @details
    #  Returns the flag to indicate the North direction is reversed.<br>
    #  True: Reverses the North direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the North direction.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    NorthDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetNorthDirectionReversed, fset = __SetNorthDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the zenith direction.
    # @details
    #  The Zenith direction property takes takes and returns a Tag from an NX object.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ZenithDirection = property(fget = __GetZenithDirection, fset = __SetZenithDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reverse Zenith direction.
    # @details
    #  Returns the flag to indicate the Zenith direction is reversed.<br>
    #  True: Reverses the Zenith direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the Zenith direction.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    ZenithDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetZenithDirectionReversed, fset = __SetZenithDirectionReversed)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_ZenithNorthSystem
    __del__ = lambda self: None
ZenithNorthSystem_swigregister = _SpeosNX.ZenithNorthSystem_swigregister
ZenithNorthSystem_swigregister(ZenithNorthSystem)

class Feature(_object):
    """
    @brief Represents a Speos feature.
    @details
     A base class for all Speos features.<br>

     This is an abstract class that provides the basic functionality common to all simulation features.<br>
     This is an abstract class, and cannot be instantiated.<br>
     To obtain an instance of this class, refer to the simulation builders.<br>
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, Feature, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, Feature, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_Feature
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def Update(self):
        """@brief Updates the feature."""
        return _SpeosNX.Feature_Update(self)


    def __GetName(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Feature___GetName(self)

    def __GetTag(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Feature___GetTag(self)

    def Delete(self):
        """@brief Deletes the feature."""
        return _SpeosNX.Feature_Delete(self)


    ##
    # @brief Returns the name of the feature.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.
    Name = property(fget = __GetName)
    ##
    # @brief Returns the NX tag for this feature.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.
    Tag = property(fget = __GetTag)

Feature_swigregister = _SpeosNX.Feature_swigregister
Feature_swigregister(Feature)

class FolderBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents a Folder Builder.
    @details
     The Folder Builder creates or edits Folder features. <br>

     To create a new instance of this class, use FeatureCollection.CreateFolderBuilder.<br>
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, FolderBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, FolderBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_FolderBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def __GetFeatures(self):
        return _SpeosNX.FolderBuilder___GetFeatures(self)

    def __SetFeatures(self, features):
        return _SpeosNX.FolderBuilder___SetFeatures(self, features)

    def Remove(self, *args):
        """
        @brief Removes the specified feature object from the folder.
        @details
         The specified feature object must be a member of the folder to be removed from it.
        @param[in] "feature" the feature object.<br>
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FolderBuilder_Remove(self, *args)


    def Add(self, feature):
        """
        @brief Adds the specified feature object into the folder.
        @param[in] "feature" the feature object.<br>
        @return True if successfully added into the folder; Otherwise, returns False.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FolderBuilder_Add(self, feature)


    def Insert(self, feature, after=None):
        """
        @brief Inserts the specified feature object into the folder after another specified feature.            
        @param[in] "feature" the feature object to add.<br>
        @param[in] "after" a feature object after which the feature object should be insert.<br>
        @return True if successfully inserted into the folder; Otherwise, returns False.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FolderBuilder_Insert(self, feature, after)


    def IsCompatible(self, feature):
        """
        @brief Checks if the specified feature object is compatible with this folder.
        @param[in] "feature" the feature object.<br>
        @return True if the specified feature object is compatible with this folder; Otherwise, returns False.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FolderBuilder_IsCompatible(self, feature)


    def __SetCategory(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.FolderBuilder___SetCategory(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets features belonging to this folder.
    # @details
    #  The Features property takes and returns a list of feature objects.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: List of Feature objects.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty list.
    Features = property(fget = __GetFeatures, fset = __SetFeatures)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the category type of the folder.
    # @details
    #  The values are: <br>
    #  0 - None.<br>
    #  1 - Properties.<br>
    #  2 - Sources.<br>
    #  3 - Sensors.<br>
    #  4 - Simulations.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</br>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is None (0). A category type other than None (0) must be defined.
    Category = property(fset = __SetCategory)

FolderBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.FolderBuilder_swigregister
FolderBuilder_swigregister(FolderBuilder)

class OpticalPropertiesBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents the builder for optical properties
    @details
     The optical properties builder is used to create and edit optical properties features.


     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateOpticalPropertiesBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, OpticalPropertiesBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, OpticalPropertiesBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_OpticalPropertiesBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def __GetOpticalPropertiesGeometry(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetOpticalPropertiesGeometry(self)

    def __GetUseOpticalProperties(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetUseOpticalProperties(self)

    def __SetUseOpticalProperties(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetUseOpticalProperties(self, value)

    def __GetVOPType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetVOPType(self)

    def __SetVOPType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetVOPType(self, value)

    def __GetVOPIndex(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetVOPIndex(self)

    def __SetVOPIndex(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetVOPIndex(self, value)

    def __GetVOPAbsorption(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetVOPAbsorption(self)

    def __SetVOPAbsorption(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetVOPAbsorption(self, value)

    def __GetUseVOPConstringence(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetUseVOPConstringence(self)

    def __SetUseVOPConstringence(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetUseVOPConstringence(self, value)

    def __GetVOPConstringence(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetVOPConstringence(self)

    def __SetVOPConstringence(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetVOPConstringence(self, value)

    def __GetVOPLibraryFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetVOPLibraryFilePath(self)

    def __SetVOPLibraryFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetVOPLibraryFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetSOPType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetSOPType(self)

    def __SetSOPType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetSOPType(self, value)

    def __GetSOPReflectance(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetSOPReflectance(self)

    def __SetSOPReflectance(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetSOPReflectance(self, value)

    def __GetSOPLibraryFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetSOPLibraryFilePath(self)

    def __SetSOPLibraryFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetSOPLibraryFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetSOPPluginFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetSOPPluginFilePath(self)

    def __SetSOPPluginFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetSOPPluginFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetSOPParametersFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetSOPParametersFilePath(self)

    def __SetSOPParametersFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetSOPParametersFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetUseMeshingProperties(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetUseMeshingProperties(self)

    def __SetUseMeshingProperties(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetUseMeshingProperties(self, value)

    def __GetAngle(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetAngle(self)

    def __SetAngle(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetAngle(self, value)

    def __GetSagMode(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetSagMode(self)

    def __SetSagMode(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetSagMode(self, value)

    def __GetSagValue(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetSagValue(self)

    def __SetSagValue(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetSagValue(self, value)

    def __GetStepMode(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetStepMode(self)

    def __SetStepMode(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetStepMode(self, value)

    def __GetStepValue(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetStepValue(self)

    def __SetStepValue(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetStepValue(self, value)

    def __GetSpecificParametersFacetEdges(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetSpecificParametersFacetEdges(self)

    def __SetSpecificParametersFacetEdges(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetSpecificParametersFacetEdges(self, value)

    def __GetMeshingEdgeSagValue(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetMeshingEdgeSagValue(self)

    def __SetMeshingEdgeSagValue(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetMeshingEdgeSagValue(self, value)

    def __GetMeshingEdgeAngle(self):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___GetMeshingEdgeAngle(self)

    def __SetMeshingEdgeAngle(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder___SetMeshingEdgeAngle(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing angle.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsMeshingProperties property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: (0.0, 90.0).<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 15.0 degrees.
    Angle = property(fget = __GetAngle, fset = __SetAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing angle.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsSpecificParametersFacetEdges property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  Defines the maximum angular variation in degrees between successive tangents for all points along a solid edge.
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: (0.0, 90.0).<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 10.0 degrees.
    MeshingEdgeAngle = property(fget = __GetMeshingEdgeAngle, fset = __SetMeshingEdgeAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing edge sag value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsSpecificParametersFacetEdges property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  Defines the maximum distance between the geometry and the meshing on the edges. The Meshing edge sag value always uses the Fixed mode.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.1 mm.
    MeshingEdgeSagValue = property(fget = __GetMeshingEdgeSagValue, fset = __SetMeshingEdgeSagValue)
    ##
    # @brief Gets optical properties geometry.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: OpticalPropertiesGeometry object.
    OpticalPropertiesGeometry = property(fget = __GetOpticalPropertiesGeometry)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the surface optical properties library file.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SOPType property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    SOPLibraryFilePath = property(fget = __GetSOPLibraryFilePath, fset = __SetSOPLibraryFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the surface optical properties parameters file.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SOPType property must be 3.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    SOPParametersFilePath = property(fget = __GetSOPParametersFilePath, fset = __SetSOPParametersFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the surface optical properties plug-in file.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SOPType property must be 3.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    SOPPluginFilePath = property(fget = __GetSOPPluginFilePath, fset = __SetSOPPluginFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the surface optical properties reflectance.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SOPType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0.0, 100.0].<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 100.0.
    SOPReflectance = property(fget = __GetSOPReflectance, fset = __SetSOPReflectance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the surface optical properties.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsOpticalProperties property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Optical Polished, uses a transparent or perfectly polished material (glass, plastic).<br>
    #  1 - Mirror, uses a perfect specular surface and edits the Reflectance value if needed.<br>
    #  2 - Library, with this value the SOPLibraryFile property is available and must be defined.<br>
    #  3 - Plug-in, selects a custom made *.sop plug-in as File and the Parameters file for the plug-in.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 1.
    SOPType = property(fget = __GetSOPType, fset = __SetSOPType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing sag mode.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsMeshingProperties property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Proportional, the value adapts and adjusts to the size of each face of the object.<br>
    #  1 - Fixed, the value will remain unchanged no matter the size or shape of the object. <br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 1.
    SagMode = property(fget = __GetSagMode, fset = __SetSagMode)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing sag value.
    # @details 
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.5 mm.
    SagValue = property(fget = __GetSagValue, fset = __SetSagValue)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the specific parameters property for facet edges.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsMeshingProperties property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  Allows you to control the precision of the meshing on the edges of the faces.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Enables specific parameters for facet edges.<br>
    #  False: Disables specific parameters for facet edges.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    SpecificParametersFacetEdges = property(fget = __GetSpecificParametersFacetEdges, fset = __SetSpecificParametersFacetEdges)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing step mode.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsMeshingProperties property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Proportional, the value adapts and adjusts to the size of each face of the object.<br>
    #  1 - Fixed, the value will remain unchanged no matter the size or shape of the object.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 1.
    StepMode = property(fget = __GetStepMode, fset = __SetStepMode)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing step value.
    # @details
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 1.0 mm.
    StepValue = property(fget = __GetStepValue, fset = __SetStepValue)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the meshing properties property.
    # @details 
    #  True: Enables meshing properties.<br>
    #  False: Disables meshing properties.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    UseMeshingProperties = property(fget = __GetUseMeshingProperties, fset = __SetUseMeshingProperties)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the optical properties property.
    # @details 
    #  True: Enables optical properties.<br>
    #  False: Disables optical properties.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean. <br>
    #  
    #  The default value is True.
    UseOpticalProperties = property(fget = __GetUseOpticalProperties, fset = __SetUseOpticalProperties)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the volume optical properties constringence property.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The VOPType property must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Enables constringence.<br>
    #  False: Disables constringence.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    UseVOPConstringence = property(fget = __GetUseVOPConstringence, fset = __SetUseVOPConstringence)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the volume optical properties absorption.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The VOPType property must be 0.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.0.
    VOPAbsorption = property(fget = __GetVOPAbsorption, fset = __SetVOPAbsorption)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the volume optical properties constringence.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsVOPConstringence property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 20.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 60.0
    VOPConstringence = property(fget = __GetVOPConstringence, fset = __SetVOPConstringence)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the volume optical properties index.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The VOPType property must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 1.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 1.5.
    VOPIndex = property(fget = __GetVOPIndex, fset = __SetVOPIndex)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the volume optical properties library file.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The VOPType property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    VOPLibraryFilePath = property(fget = __GetVOPLibraryFilePath, fset = __SetVOPLibraryFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the volume optical properties type.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsOpticalProperties property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Optic, uses transparent colorless part without bulk scattering.<br>
    #  1 - Opaque (Solid Body), uses non transparent part.<br>
    #  2 - Library, with this value the VOPLibraryFile property is available and must be defined.<br>
    #  3 - None, does not apply a volume optical properties on surface in case you have a surface geometry.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 1.
    VOPType = property(fget = __GetVOPType, fset = __SetVOPType)

OpticalPropertiesBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.OpticalPropertiesBuilder_swigregister
OpticalPropertiesBuilder_swigregister(OpticalPropertiesBuilder)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the sensor type.
    # @details 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Photometric. The sensor considers the visible spectrum.<br>
    #  1 - Radiometric. The sensor considers the entire spectrum.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    Type = property(fget = __GetType, fset = __SetType)
    ##
