class Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents the builder for a 3D irradiance sensor.
    @details
     The 3D irradiance sensor builder is used to create and edit 3D irradiance sensor features.


     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSensor3DIrradianceBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetMeasureType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetMeasureType(self)

    def __SetMeasureType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetMeasureType(self, value)

    def __GetUseRayFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetUseRayFile(self)

    def __SetUseRayFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetUseRayFile(self, value)

    def __GetRayFileFormat(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetRayFileFormat(self)

    def __SetRayFileFormat(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetRayFileFormat(self, value)

    def __GetIntegrationType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetIntegrationType(self)

    def __SetIntegrationType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetIntegrationType(self, value)

    def __GetSelections(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetSelections(self)

    def __SetSelections(self, tags):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetSelections(self, tags)

    def __GetLayer(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetLayer(self)

    def __SetLayer(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetLayer(self, value)

    def __GetReflection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetReflection(self)

    def __SetReflection(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetReflection(self, value)

    def __GetTransmission(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetTransmission(self)

    def __SetTransmission(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetTransmission(self, value)

    def __GetAbsorption(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetAbsorption(self)

    def __SetAbsorption(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetAbsorption(self, value)

    def __GetUseTemplateFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetUseTemplateFile(self)

    def __SetUseTemplateFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetUseTemplateFile(self, value)

    def __GetTemplateFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetTemplateFilePath(self)

    def __SetTemplateFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetTemplateFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetWavelengthStart(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetWavelengthStart(self)

    def __SetWavelengthStart(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetWavelengthStart(self, value)

    def __GetWavelengthEnd(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetWavelengthEnd(self)

    def __SetWavelengthEnd(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetWavelengthEnd(self, value)

    def __GetWavelengthSampling(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetWavelengthSampling(self)

    def __SetWavelengthSampling(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___SetWavelengthSampling(self, value)

    def __GetWavelengthResolution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder___GetWavelengthResolution(self)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the absorption property.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The property MeasureType must be 0 or 2, and IntegrationType must be 0.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    Absorption = property(fget = __GetAbsorption, fset = __SetAbsorption)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the integration type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Planar. Integration that is made orthogonally with the sensor plan.<br>
    #  1 - Radial. Follows specific street lighting illumination regulations.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    IntegrationType = property(fget = __GetIntegrationType, fset = __SetIntegrationType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the layer mode.
    # @details 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - None.<br>
    #  1 - Source.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    Layer = property(fget = __GetLayer, fset = __SetLayer)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the measure type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Photometric to compute the luminous intensity and generate an extended map for Virtual 3D Photometric Lab.<br>
    #  1 - Colorimetric to compute the radiant intensity and generate an extended map for Virtual 3D Photometric Lab.<br>
    #  2 - Radiometric to compute the color results without any spectral layer separation and generate a spectral map for Virtual 3D Photometric Lab.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    MeasureType = property(fget = __GetMeasureType, fset = __SetMeasureType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ray file format.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseRayFile property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  Defines the type of ray file. The simulation creates the ray file.<br>
    # 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Speos without Polarization.<br>
    #  1 - Speos with Polarization.<br>
    #  2 - IES TM-25 without Polarization.<br>
    #  3 - IES TM-25 with Polarization.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    RayFileFormat = property(fget = __GetRayFileFormat, fset = __SetRayFileFormat)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reflection property.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The property MeasureType must be 0 or 2, and IntegrationType must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is True.
    Reflection = property(fget = __GetReflection, fset = __SetReflection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the selected faces or bodies.
    # @details 
    #  The Selections property takes and returns a list of feature tags.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: List of integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty list.
    Selections = property(fget = __GetSelections, fset = __SetSelections)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the XM3 template file.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The property TemplateFile must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    TemplateFilePath = property(fget = __GetTemplateFilePath, fset = __SetTemplateFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the transmission property.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The property MeasureType must be 0 or 2, and IntegrationType must be 0.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    Transmission = property(fget = __GetTransmission, fset = __SetTransmission)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable or disable use of ray file.
    # @details 
    #  True: Uses ray file.<br>
    #  False: Does not use ray file.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    UseRayFile = property(fget = __GetUseRayFile, fset = __SetUseRayFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable or disable use of XM3 template file.
    # @details
    #  True: Uses XM3 template file.<br>
    #  False: Does not use XM3 template file.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    UseTemplateFile = property(fget = __GetUseTemplateFile, fset = __SetUseTemplateFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the higher value of the wavelength range to be considered by the sensor.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The property MeasureType must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  The sensor does not take into account wavelengths beyond the borders that you define.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in nm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 700.0 nm.
    WavelengthEnd = property(fget = __GetWavelengthEnd, fset = __SetWavelengthEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the Wavelength resolution.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The property MeasureType must be 1.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    WavelengthResolution = property(fget = __GetWavelengthResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the wavelength sampling.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The property MeasureType must be 1.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 13.
    WavelengthSampling = property(fget = __GetWavelengthSampling, fset = __SetWavelengthSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the lower value of the wavelength range to be considered by the sensor.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The property MeasureType must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  The sensor does not take into account wavelengths beyond the borders that you define.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in nm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 400.0 nm.
    WavelengthStart = property(fget = __GetWavelengthStart, fset = __SetWavelengthStart)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None
Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder_swigregister
Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder_swigregister(Sensor3DIrradianceBuilder)

class SensorCommonBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief A base class for all Sensor Builders.
    @details
     A Builder is an object that is used to create and edit Features.

     This is an abstract class that provides the basic functionality common to all builders. See the Builder subclasses for details of application-specific builders.

     This is an abstract class, and cannot be instantiated.
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SensorCommonBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SensorCommonBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SensorCommonBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def __GetType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetType(self)

    def __SetType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetType(self, value)

    def __GetAxisSystem(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetAxisSystem(self)

    def __GetXStart(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetXStart(self)

    def __SetXStart(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetXStart(self, value)

    def __GetXEnd(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetXEnd(self)

    def __SetXEnd(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetXEnd(self, value)

    def __GetXSampling(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetXSampling(self)

    def __SetXSampling(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetXSampling(self, value)

    def __GetXResolution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetXResolution(self)

    def __SetXResolution(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetXResolution(self, value)

    def __GetXMirroredExtent(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetXMirroredExtent(self)

    def __SetXMirroredExtent(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetXMirroredExtent(self, value)

    def __GetYStart(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetYStart(self)

    def __SetYStart(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetYStart(self, value)

    def __GetYEnd(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetYEnd(self)

    def __SetYEnd(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetYEnd(self, value)

    def __GetYSampling(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetYSampling(self)

    def __SetYSampling(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetYSampling(self, value)

    def __GetYResolution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetYResolution(self)

    def __SetYResolution(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetYResolution(self, value)

    def __GetYMirroredExtent(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetYMirroredExtent(self)

    def __SetYMirroredExtent(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetYMirroredExtent(self, value)

    def __GetWavelengthStart(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetWavelengthStart(self)

    def __SetWavelengthStart(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetWavelengthStart(self, value)

    def __GetWavelengthEnd(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetWavelengthEnd(self)

    def __SetWavelengthEnd(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetWavelengthEnd(self, value)

    def __GetWavelengthSampling(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetWavelengthSampling(self)

    def __SetWavelengthSampling(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetWavelengthSampling(self, value)

    def __GetWavelengthResolution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetWavelengthResolution(self)

    def __SetWavelengthResolution(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetWavelengthResolution(self, value)

    def __GetUseTemplateFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetUseTemplateFile(self)

    def __SetUseTemplateFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetUseTemplateFile(self, value)

    def __GetDimensionFromFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetDimensionFromFile(self)

    def __SetDimensionFromFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetDimensionFromFile(self, value)

    def __GetDisplayPropertiesFromFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetDisplayPropertiesFromFile(self)

    def __SetDisplayPropertiesFromFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetDisplayPropertiesFromFile(self, value)

    def IsTemplateFileValid(self):
        """
        @brief Checks whether the template file is valid.
        @returns 
         True: The template file is valid.<br>
         False: The template file is not valid.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder_IsTemplateFileValid(self)


    def __GetTemplateFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetTemplateFilePath(self)

    def __SetTemplateFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetTemplateFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetTemplateType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetTemplateType(self)

    def __GetSensorFilter(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetSensorFilter(self)

    def __GetShowGrid(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetShowGrid(self)

    def __SetShowGrid(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetShowGrid(self, value)

    def __GetGridOriginX(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetGridOriginX(self)

    def __SetGridOriginX(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetGridOriginX(self, value)

    def __GetGridOriginY(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetGridOriginY(self)

    def __SetGridOriginY(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetGridOriginY(self, value)

    def __GetGridStepX(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetGridStepX(self)

    def __SetGridStepX(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetGridStepX(self, value)

    def __GetGridStepY(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___GetGridStepY(self)

    def __SetGridStepY(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder___SetGridStepY(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets the Axis System of the Sensor.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: AxisSystem object.
    AxisSystem = property(fget = __GetAxisSystem)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable the use of dimensions that come from File
    # @details
    #  True: Uses the following values from the XMP template: type, X and Y size, Wavelength values.<br>
    #  False: Does not use the dimension from file.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    DimensionFromFile = property(fget = __GetDimensionFromFile, fset = __SetDimensionFromFile)
    ##
    # @brief  Gets or sets the property to enable the use of display properties that come from File.
    # @details
    #  True: Uses all the grid related values from the .xml file.<br>
    #  False: Does not use the Display properties from file.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    DisplayPropertiesFromFile = property(fget = __GetDisplayPropertiesFromFile, fset = __SetDisplayPropertiesFromFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the grid X origin
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.0.
    GridOriginX = property(fget = __GetGridOriginX, fset = __SetGridOriginX)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the grid Y origin
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.0.
    GridOriginY = property(fget = __GetGridOriginY, fset = __SetGridOriginY)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the grid X step
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 10.0.
    GridStepX = property(fget = __GetGridStepX, fset = __SetGridStepX)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the grid Y step
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 10.0.
    GridStepY = property(fget = __GetGridStepY, fset = __SetGridStepY)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the sensor filter
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: SensorFilter object.
    SensorFilter = property(fget = __GetSensorFilter)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable grid preview.
    # @details
    #  True: Displays a grid on the sensor.<br>
    #  False: Does not display a grid on the sensor.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is True.
    ShowGrid = property(fget = __GetShowGrid, fset = __SetShowGrid)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the template file's path.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    TemplateFilePath = property(fget = __GetTemplateFilePath, fset = __SetTemplateFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the template type
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - None<br>
    #  1 - Measure<br>
    #  2 - Template <br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    TemplateType = property(fget = __GetTemplateType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the type of the sensor.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Photometric, results in cd.<br>
    #  1 - Colorimetric, color results in cd or W/sr.<br>
    #  2 - Radiometric, results in W/sr.<br>
    #  3 - Spectral, results in cd or W/sr.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    Type = property(fget = __GetType, fset = __SetType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable the use of template file
    # @details 
    #  True: Enables Template File. <br>
    #  False: Disables Template File. <br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.
    UseTemplateFile = property(fget = __GetUseTemplateFile, fset = __SetUseTemplateFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the wavelength ending border.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Type property must be 1 or 3.<br>
    #  
    #  The sensor does not take account wavelengths beyond the borders that you define.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in nm).<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 700.0 nm.
    WavelengthEnd = property(fget = __GetWavelengthEnd, fset = __SetWavelengthEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Wavelength resolution
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Type property must be 1 or 3.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    WavelengthResolution = property(fget = __GetWavelengthResolution, fset = __SetWavelengthResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the wavelength sampling.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Type property must be 1 or 3.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 13.
    WavelengthSampling = property(fget = __GetWavelengthSampling, fset = __SetWavelengthSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the wavelength starting border.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Type property must be 1 or 3.<br>
    #  
    #  The sensor does not take account wavelengths beyond the borders that you define.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in nm).<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 400.0 nm.
    WavelengthStart = property(fget = __GetWavelengthStart, fset = __SetWavelengthStart)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sensor X end dimension value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 50.0 mm.
    XEnd = property(fget = __GetXEnd, fset = __SetXEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the Sensor X dimension mirrored extent value.
    # @details 
    #  True: XStart == -XEnd, you can only change the XEnd value.<br>
    #  False: XStart and XEnd can have different value.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    XMirroredExtent = property(fget = __GetXMirroredExtent, fset = __SetXMirroredExtent)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sensor X dimension resolution value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.
    XResolution = property(fget = __GetXResolution, fset = __SetXResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sensor X dimension sampling value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 100.
    XSampling = property(fget = __GetXSampling, fset = __SetXSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sensor X start dimension value.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is -50.0 mm.
    XStart = property(fget = __GetXStart, fset = __SetXStart)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sensor Y end dimension value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 50.0 mm.
    YEnd = property(fget = __GetYEnd, fset = __SetYEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the Sensor Y dimension mirrored extent value.
    # @details
    #  True: YStart == -YEnd, you can only change the YEnd value.<br>
    #  False: YStart and YEnd can have different value.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    YMirroredExtent = property(fget = __GetYMirroredExtent, fset = __SetYMirroredExtent)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sensor Y dimension resolution value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.
    YResolution = property(fget = __GetYResolution, fset = __SetYResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sensor Y dimension sampling value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    YSampling = property(fget = __GetYSampling, fset = __SetYSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sensor Y start dimension value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is -50.0 mm.
    YStart = property(fget = __GetYStart, fset = __SetYStart)

SensorCommonBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SensorCommonBuilder_swigregister
SensorCommonBuilder_swigregister(SensorCommonBuilder)

    """
    @brief Represents the builder for an observer sensor.
    @details
     The observer sensor builder is used to create and edit observer sensor features.


     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSensorObserverBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SensorObserverBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SensorObserverBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SensorObserverBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    #

    AutoFramingHorizontal = property(fget = __GetAutoFramingHorizontal, fset = __SetAutoFramingHorizontal)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the automatic framing horizontal position.

    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>

    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is -50.0 mm.
    DimensionVerticalStart = property(fget = __GetDimensionVerticalStart, fset = __SetDimensionVerticalStart)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the distance.
    # @details 
    #  Adjusts the radius of the sphere to narrow or widen the global field of vision.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 1000.0 mm.
    Distance = property(fget = __GetDistance, fset = __SetDistance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the focal.
    # @details 
    #  Adjusts the distance between the sensor radiance plan and the origin point of the observed object. The larger the focal, the closer to the object.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 50.0 mm.
    Focal = property(fget = __GetFocal, fset = __SetFocal)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the integration angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 5.0 degrees.
    IntegrationAngle = property(fget = __GetIntegrationAngle, fset = __SetIntegrationAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the interocular distance.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Stereo property must be True.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.
    # 
    #  The default value is 65.0 mm.
    InterocularDistance = property(fget = __GetInterocularDistance, fset = __SetInterocularDistance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the layer mode.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - None, the simulation generates a Speos360 file with one layer for all sources.<br>
    #  1 - Source, the result includes one layer per active source.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    Layer = property(fget = __GetLayer, fset = __SetLayer)
    ##
    # @brief gets or sets the stereo property.
    # @details
    #  When you define a stereo sensor, make sure that the Front direction is horizontal, the Top direction is vertical, and the Central resolution matches the intended 3D display.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Enables stereo.<br>
    #  False: Disables stereo.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    Stereo = property(fget = __GetStereo, fset = __SetStereo)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the horizontal end for vision field.
    # @details
    #  Vision Field corresponds to the surface on which are located observer positions around target point.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [-180.0, 180.0]<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 180.0 degrees.
    VisionFieldHorizontalEnd = property(fget = __GetVisionFieldHorizontalEnd, fset = __SetVisionFieldHorizontalEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the mirrored extent property for horizontal vision field.
    # @details
    #  Vision Field corresponds to the surface on which are located observer positions around target point.<br>
    #  
    #  True: VisionFieldHorizontalStart == -VisionFieldHorizontalEnd, you can only change the VisionFieldHorizontalEnd value.<br>
    #  False: VisionFieldHorizontalStart and VisionFieldHorizontalEnd can have different value.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    VisionFieldHorizontalMirroredExtent = property(fget = __GetVisionFieldHorizontalMirroredExtent, fset = __SetVisionFieldHorizontalMirroredExtent)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the horizontal resolution for vision field.
    # @details
    #  Vision Field corresponds to the surface on which are located observer positions around target point.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    VisionFieldHorizontalResolution = property(fget = __GetVisionFieldHorizontalResolution, fset = __SetVisionFieldHorizontalResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the horizontal sampling for vision field.
    # @details
    #  Vision Field corresponds to the surface on which are located observer positions around target point.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #           
    #  The default value is 9.
    VisionFieldHorizontalSampling = property(fget = __GetVisionFieldHorizontalSampling, fset = __SetVisionFieldHorizontalSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the horizontal start for vision field.
    # @details 
    #  Vision Field corresponds to the surface on which are located observer positions around target point.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [-180.0, 180.0]<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is -180.0 degrees.
    VisionFieldHorizontalStart = property(fget = __GetVisionFieldHorizontalStart, fset = __SetVisionFieldHorizontalStart)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the vertical end for vision field.
    # @details
    #  Vision Field corresponds to the surface on which are located observer positions around target point.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [-90.0, 90.0]<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 90.0 degrees.
    VisionFieldVerticalEnd = property(fget = __GetVisionFieldVerticalEnd, fset = __SetVisionFieldVerticalEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the mirrored extent property for vertical vision field.
    # @details
    #  Vision Field corresponds to the surface on which are located observer positions around target point.<br>
    # 
    #  True: VisionFieldVerticalStart == -VisionFieldVerticalEnd, you can only change the VisionFieldVerticalEnd value.<br>
    #  False: VisionFieldVerticalStart and VisionFieldVerticalEnd can have different value.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    VisionFieldVerticalMirroredExtent = property(fget = __GetVisionFieldVerticalMirroredExtent, fset = __SetVisionFieldVerticalMirroredExtent)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the vertical resolution for vision field.
    # @details
    #  Vision Field corresponds to the surface on which are located observer positions around target point. <br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    VisionFieldVerticalResolution = property(fget = __GetVisionFieldVerticalResolution, fset = __SetVisionFieldVerticalResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the vertical sampling for vision field.
    # @details
    #  Vision Field corresponds to the surface on which are located observer positions around target point.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #           
    #  The default value is 5.
    VisionFieldVerticalSampling = property(fget = __GetVisionFieldVerticalSampling, fset = __SetVisionFieldVerticalSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the vertical start for vision field.
    # @details
    #  Vision Field corresponds to the surface on which are located observer positions around target point. <br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [-90.0, 90.0]<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is -90.0 degrees.
    VisionFieldVerticalStart = property(fget = __GetVisionFieldVerticalStart, fset = __SetVisionFieldVerticalStart)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the higher value of the wavelength range to be considered by the sensor.
    # @details
    #  The sensor does not take into account wavelengths beyond the borders that you define.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in nm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 700.0 nm.
    WavelengthEnd = property(fget = __GetWavelengthEnd, fset = __SetWavelengthEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Wavelength resolution
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    WavelengthResolution = property(fget = __GetWavelengthResolution, fset = __SetWavelengthResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the wavelength sampling.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 13.
    WavelengthSampling = property(fget = __GetWavelengthSampling, fset = __SetWavelengthSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the lower value of the wavelength range to be considered by the sensor.
    # @details
    #  The sensor does not take into account wavelengths beyond the borders that you define.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in nm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 400.0 nm.
    WavelengthStart = property(fget = __GetWavelengthStart, fset = __SetWavelengthStart)

SensorObserverBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SensorObserverBuilder_swigregister
SensorObserverBuilder_swigregister(SensorObserverBuilder)

        return _SpeosNX.SensorVRImmersiveBuilder___GetIntegrationAngle(self)

    def __SetIntegrationAngle(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorVRImmersiveBuilder___SetIntegrationAngle(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the automatic framing property.
    # @details 
    #  True: Activates automatic framing.<br>
    #  False: Deactivates automatic framing.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    ActivateAutomaticFraming = property(fget = __GetActivateAutomaticFraming, fset = __SetActivateAutomaticFraming)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the axis system.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: AxisSytem object.
    AxisSystem = property(fget = __GetAxisSystem)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the back face property.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables back face in the simulation.<br>
    #  False: Disables back face in the simulation.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    Back = property(fget = __GetBack, fset = __SetBack)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the bottom face property.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables bottom face in the simulation.<br>
    #  False: Disables bottom face in the simulation.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    Bottom = property(fget = __GetBottom, fset = __SetBottom)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the framing face.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnableFraming property must be True.<br>
    #  Positions the camera, in the 3D view, according to the faces selected from the choice list.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - FRONT.<br>
    #  1 - BACK.<br>
    #  2 - TOP.<br>
    #  3 - BOTTOM.<br>
    #  4 - LEFT.<br>
    #  5 - RIGHT.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    FramingFace = property(fget = __GetFramingFace, fset = __SetFramingFace)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the front face property.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables front face in the simulation.<br>
    #  False: Disables front face in the simulation.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is True.
    Front = property(fget = __GetFront, fset = __SetFront)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the integration angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 5.0 degrees.
    IntegrationAngle = property(fget = __GetIntegrationAngle, fset = __SetIntegrationAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the interocular distance.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Stereo property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.
    #  
    #  The default value is 65.0 mm.
    InterocularDistance = property(fget = __GetInterocularDistance, fset = __SetInterocularDistance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the layer mode.
    # @details 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - None, the simulation generates a Speos360 file with one layer for all sources.<br>
    #  1 - Source, the result includes one layer per active source.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    Layer = property(fget = __GetLayer, fset = __SetLayer)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the left face property.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables left face in the simulation.<br>
    #  False: Disables left face in the simulation.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    Left = property(fget = __GetLeft, fset = __SetLeft)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the preview arrows size.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in nm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 500.0 nm.
    PreviewSize = property(fget = __GetPreviewSize, fset = __SetPreviewSize)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the resolution.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.
    Resolution = property(fget = __GetResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the right face property.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables right face in the simulation.<br>
    #  False: Disables right face in the simulation.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    Right = property(fget = __GetRight, fset = __SetRight)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the sampling.
    # @details 
    #   Edits the value to compute the resolution of the result.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 600.
    Sampling = property(fget = __GetSampling, fset = __SetSampling)
    ##
    # @brief gets or sets the stereo property.
    # @details 
    #  When you define a stereo sensor, make sure that the Front direction is horizontal, the Top direction is vertical, and the Central resolution matches the intended 3D display.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Enables stereo.<br>
    #  False: Disables stereo.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #

    # @details

    #

    Top = property(fget = __GetTop, fset = __SetTop)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the higher value of the wavelength range to be considered by the sensor.
    # @details

class SimulationCommonBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief A base class for all Simulation Builders.
    @details
     A Builder is an object that is used to create and edit Features.

     This is an abstract class that provides the basic functionality common to all builders. See the Builder subclasses for details of application-specific builders.

     This is an abstract class, and cannot be instantiated.
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SimulationCommonBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SimulationCommonBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SimulationCommonBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def __GetFeatureSimulation(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetFeatureSimulation(self)

    def __GetSources(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetSources(self)

    def AddSources(self, sources):
        """
        @brief Adds sources into the simulation.
        @param[in] "sources" : List of Feature object 
        @return void.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder_AddSources(self, sources)


    def RemoveSources(self, sources):
        """
        @brief Deletes sources from the simulation.
        @param[in] "sources" : List of Feature object
        @return void.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder_RemoveSources(self, sources)


    def __GetGeometries(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetGeometries(self)

    def AddGeometries(self, tags):
        """
        @brief Adds geometries into the simulation.
        @details
         The AddGeometries function takes a list of feature tag as parameter. 
        @param[in] "tags" : List of integer.
        @return void.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder_AddGeometries(self, tags)


    def RemoveGeometries(self, tags):
        """
        @brief Deletes geometries from the simulation.
        @details
         The DeleteGeometries function takes a list of feature tag as parameter.
        @param[in] "tags" : List of integer.
        @return void.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder_RemoveGeometries(self, tags)


    def __GetSensors(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetSensors(self)

    def AddSensors(self, sensors):
        """
        @brief Adds sensors into the simulation.
        @param[in] "sensors" : List of Feature object.
        @return void.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder_AddSensors(self, sensors)


    def RemoveSensors(self, sensors):
        """
        @brief Deletes sensors from the simulation.
        @param[in] "sensors" : List of Feature object.
        @return void.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder_RemoveSensors(self, sensors)


    def __GetEstimatedRam(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetEstimatedRam(self)

    def __GetLightExpert(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetLightExpert(self)

    def __SetLightExpert(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___SetLightExpert(self, value)

    def __GetAmbientMaterial(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetAmbientMaterial(self)

    def __SetAmbientMaterial(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___SetAmbientMaterial(self, value)

    def __GetSelectAmbientMaterial(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetSelectAmbientMaterial(self)

    def __SetSelectAmbientMaterial(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___SetSelectAmbientMaterial(self, tag)

    def __GetStandardDeviation(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetStandardDeviation(self)

    def __SetStandardDeviation(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___SetStandardDeviation(self, value)

    def __GetUsePresetSettings(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetUsePresetSettings(self)

    def __SetUsePresetSettings(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___SetUsePresetSettings(self, value)

    def __GetPreset(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetPreset(self)

    def __SetPreset(self, preset):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___SetPreset(self, preset)

    def __GetAllPreset(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetAllPreset(self)

    def __GetSettings(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___GetSettings(self)

    def __SetSettings(self, settings):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationCommonBuilder___SetSettings(self, settings)

    ##
    # @brief Gets all Preset.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: List of Preset object.
    AllPreset = property(fget = __GetAllPreset)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable ambient material.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables Ambient Material.<br>
    #  False: Disables Ambient Material.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    AmbientMaterial = property(fget = __GetAmbientMaterial, fset = __SetAmbientMaterial)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the estimated RAM usage.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.
    EstimatedRam = property(fget = __GetEstimatedRam)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the simulation feature object.
    # @details 
    #  Gets the simulation feature in order to launch simulations.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: FeatureSimulation object.
    FeatureSimulation = property(fget = __GetFeatureSimulation)
    ##
    # @brief Gets geometries tag.
    # @details
    #  The Geometries property returns a list of feature tag.
    # @return List of integer.
    Geometries = property(fget = __GetGeometries)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable Light Expert.

    #  True: Enables Light Expert.<br>

    #

    LightExpert = property(fget = __GetLightExpert, fset = __SetLightExpert)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Preset object.
    # @details 
    #  A preset is a predefined set of the general simulation settings.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Preset object.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is None.
    Preset = property(fget = __GetPreset, fset = __SetPreset)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the ambient material.
    # @details 
    #  The SelectedAmbientMaterial property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    SelectAmbientMaterial = property(fget = __GetSelectAmbientMaterial, fset = __SetSelectAmbientMaterial)
    ##
    # @brief Gets sensor features.
    # @details
    #  Gets the current sensor features that are in the simulation.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>:  List of Feature object.
    Sensors = property(fget = __GetSensors)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the simulation settings.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: SimulationSettings object.
    Settings = property(fget = __GetSettings, fset = __SetSettings)
    ##
    # @brief Gets source features.
    # @details 
    #  Gets the current source features that are in the simulation.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: List of Feature object.
    Sources = property(fget = __GetSources)
    StandardDeviation = property(fget = __GetStandardDeviation, fset = __SetStandardDeviation)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable preset settings.
    # @details
    #  True: Enable Preset Settings<br>
    #  False: Disable Preset Settings<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    UsePresetSettings = property(fget = __GetUsePresetSettings, fset = __SetUsePresetSettings)

class SourceAmbientCommonBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief A base class for all Ambient Source Builders.
    @details
     A Builder is an object that is used to create and edit Features.

     This is an abstract class that provides the basic functionality common to all builders. See the Builder subclasses for details of application-specific builders.

     This is an abstract class, and cannot be instantiated.
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SourceAmbientCommonBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SourceAmbientCommonBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr


    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceAmbientCommonBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None
SourceAmbientCommonBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientCommonBuilder_swigregister
SourceAmbientCommonBuilder_swigregister(SourceAmbientCommonBuilder)

class SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents the builder for an ambient environment source.
    @details
     The ambient environment source builder is used to create and edit ambient environment source features.


     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetLuminance(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetLuminance(self)

    def __SetLuminance(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetLuminance(self, value)

    def __GetImageFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetImageFilePath(self)

    def __SetImageFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetImageFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetGroundOrigin(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetGroundOrigin(self)

    def __SetGroundOrigin(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetGroundOrigin(self, tag)

    def __GetHeight(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetHeight(self)

    def __SetHeight(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetHeight(self, value)

    def __GetZenithNorthSystem(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetZenithNorthSystem(self)

    def __GetColorSpace(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetColorSpace(self)

    def __SetColorSpace(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetColorSpace(self, value)

    def __GetWhitePointType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetWhitePointType(self)

    def __SetWhitePointType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetWhitePointType(self, value)

    def __GetWhitePointX(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetWhitePointX(self)

    def __SetWhitePointX(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetWhitePointX(self, value)

    def __GetWhitePointY(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetWhitePointY(self)

    def __SetWhitePointY(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetWhitePointY(self, value)

    def __GetRedSpectrumFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetRedSpectrumFile(self)

    def __SetRedSpectrumFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetRedSpectrumFile(self, value)

    def __GetGreenSpectrumFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetGreenSpectrumFile(self)

    def __SetGreenSpectrumFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetGreenSpectrumFile(self, value)

    def __GetBlueSpectrumFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetBlueSpectrumFile(self)

    def __SetBlueSpectrumFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetBlueSpectrumFile(self, value)

    def __GetPreviewSize(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___GetPreviewSize(self)

    def __SetPreviewSize(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder___SetPreviewSize(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the blue spectrum file.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The ColorSpace property must be 2.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    BlueSpectrumFile = property(fget = __GetBlueSpectrumFile, fset = __SetBlueSpectrumFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the color space model type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - sRGB. Uses the standard and most commonly used RGB based model.<br>
    #  1 - Adobe RGB. Uses a larger gamut.<br>
    #  2 - User Defined RGB. Defines manually the white point of the standard illuminant.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ColorSpace = property(fget = __GetColorSpace, fset = __SetColorSpace)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the green spectrum file.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The ColorSpace property must be 2.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    GreenSpectrumFile = property(fget = __GetGreenSpectrumFile, fset = __SetGreenSpectrumFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ground origin.
    # @details 
    #  The GroundOrigin property takes a feature tag.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    GroundOrigin = property(fget = __GetGroundOrigin, fset = __SetGroundOrigin)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the height.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.0 mm.
    Height = property(fget = __GetHeight, fset = __SetHeight)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the image file.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    ImageFilePath = property(fget = __GetImageFilePath, fset = __SetImageFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the luminance.
    # @details
    #  The luminance parameter is the source luminance for the white point in front direction of the source.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (cd/m2).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 1000.0 cd/m2.
    Luminance = property(fget = __GetLuminance, fset = __SetLuminance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the preview arrows size.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 100.0 mm.
    PreviewSize = property(fget = __GetPreviewSize, fset = __SetPreviewSize)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the red spectrum file.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The WhitePoint property must be 4.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    RedSpectrumFile = property(fget = __GetRedSpectrumFile, fset = __SetRedSpectrumFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the white point type of the standard illuminant.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The ColorSpace property must be 2.<br>
    # 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - D65. Uses a standard daylight illuminant that provides accurate color perception and evaluation.<br>
    #  1 - D50. Uses a natural, horizon light.<br>
    #  2 - C. Uses an average daylight illuminant.<br>
    #  3 - E. Uses an illuminant that gives equal weight to all wavelengths.<br>
    #  4 - User defined. Allows to edit the Color Coordinates of the white point.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    WhitePointType = property(fget = __GetWhitePointType, fset = __SetWhitePointType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the X coordinate of the white point.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The WhitePoint property must be 4.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.31271.
    WhitePointX = property(fget = __GetWhitePointX, fset = __SetWhitePointX)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Y coordinate of the white point.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The WhitePoint property must be 4.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.32902.
    WhitePointY = property(fget = __GetWhitePointY, fset = __SetWhitePointY)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the zenith north axis system.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: ZenithNorthSystem object.
    ZenithNorthSystem = property(fget = __GetZenithNorthSystem)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None
SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder_swigregister
SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder_swigregister(SourceAmbientEnvironmentBuilder)

    def __GetWhitePointX(self):
