    def __SetWhitePointX(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___SetWhitePointX(self, value)

    def __GetWhitePointY(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___GetWhitePointY(self)

    def __SetWhitePointY(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___SetWhitePointY(self, value)

    def __GetRedSpectrumFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___GetRedSpectrumFilePath(self)

    def __SetRedSpectrumFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___SetRedSpectrumFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetGreenSpectrumFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___GetGreenSpectrumFilePath(self)

    def __SetGreenSpectrumFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___SetGreenSpectrumFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetBlueSpectrumFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___GetBlueSpectrumFilePath(self)

    def __SetBlueSpectrumFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___SetBlueSpectrumFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetNumberOfRays(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___GetNumberOfRays(self)

    def __SetNumberOfRays(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___SetNumberOfRays(self, value)

    def __GetRayLength(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___GetRayLength(self)

    def __SetRayLength(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___SetRayLength(self, value)

    def __GetShowIntensityDistribution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___GetShowIntensityDistribution(self)

    def __SetShowIntensityDistribution(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___SetShowIntensityDistribution(self, value)

    def __GetShowImage(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___GetShowImage(self)

    def __SetShowImage(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder___SetShowImage(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets the axis system.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: AxisSystem object.
    AxisSystem = property(fget = __GetAxisSystem)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the blue spectrum file.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The ColorSpace property must be 2.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    BlueSpectrumFilePath = property(fget = __GetBlueSpectrumFilePath, fset = __SetBlueSpectrumFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the color space model type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - sRGB. Uses the standard and most commonly used RGB based model.<br>
    #  1 - Adobe RGB. Uses a larger gamut.<br>
    #  2 - User Defined RGB. Defines manually the white point of the standard illuminant.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    ColorSpace = property(fget = __GetColorSpace, fset = __SetColorSpace)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the contrast ratio.
    # @details 
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IsInfiniteContrast property must be False.<br>
    #  
    #  Contrast Ratio = (Luminance of the brightest color-Luminance of the darkest color)/(Luminance of the darkest color).<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 500.
    Contrast = property(fget = __GetContrast, fset = __SetContrast)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the N value for Cos distribution.
    # @details 
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 3.0.
    CosN = property(fget = __GetCosN, fset = __SetCosN)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the FWHM angle value for Symmetric Gaussian distribution.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0.0, 180.0].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 30.0 degrees.
    GaussianFWHMAngle = property(fget = __GetGaussianFWHMAngle, fset = __SetGaussianFWHMAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the FWHM X angle value for Asymmetric Gaussian distribution.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 3.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0.0, 180.0].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 30.0 degrees.
    GaussianFWHMAngleX = property(fget = __GetGaussianFWHMAngleX, fset = __SetGaussianFWHMAngleX)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the FWHM Y angle value for Asymmetric Gaussian distribution.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 3.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0.0, 180.0].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 30.0 degrees.
    GaussianFWHMAngleY = property(fget = __GetGaussianFWHMAngleY, fset = __SetGaussianFWHMAngleY)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the green spectrum file.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The ColorSpace property must be 2.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    GreenSpectrumFilePath = property(fget = __GetGreenSpectrumFilePath, fset = __SetGreenSpectrumFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the image file.
    # @details 
    #  Selects a .jpg or a .png file.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    ImageFilePath = property(fget = __GetImageFilePath, fset = __SetImageFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable infinite contrast ratio.
    # @details 
    #  True: Enable contrast ratio.<br>
    #  False: Disable contrast ratio.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is True.
    InfiniteContrast = property(fget = __GetInfiniteContrast, fset = __SetInfiniteContrast)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the intensity file for Library distribution.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 4.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    IntensityFilePath = property(fget = __GetIntensityFilePath, fset = __SetIntensityFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the intensity diagram.
    # @details
    #  The intensity diagram of a source describes in which directions is made the emission.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Lambertian.<br>
    #  1 - Cos.<br>
    #  2 - Symmetric Gaussian.<br>
    #  3 - Asymmetric Gaussian.<br>
    #  4 - Library.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    IntensityType = property(fget = __GetIntensityType, fset = __SetIntensityType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the theta value for Lambertian distribution.
    # @details 
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0.0, 180.0].<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 180.0 degrees.
    LambertianMaximumAngle = property(fget = __GetLambertianMaximumAngle, fset = __SetLambertianMaximumAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the luminance.
    # @details 
    #  The luminance parameter is the source luminance for the white point in front direction of the source.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in cd/m2).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 50.0 cd/m2.
    Luminance = property(fget = __GetLuminance, fset = __SetLuminance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the number of rays.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 100.
    NumberOfRays = property(fget = __GetNumberOfRays, fset = __SetNumberOfRays)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ray length.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 75.0 mm.
    RayLength = property(fget = __GetRayLength, fset = __SetRayLength)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the red spectrum file.
    # @details 
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The ColorSpace property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    RedSpectrumFilePath = property(fget = __GetRedSpectrumFilePath, fset = __SetRedSpectrumFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to show the image.
    # @details
    #  True: Shows the image.<br>
    #  False: Does not show the image.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    ShowImage = property(fget = __GetShowImage, fset = __SetShowImage)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to show the intensity distribution in the 3D view.
    # @details 
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 4.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Shows the intensity distribution in the 3D view.<br>
    #  False: Does not show the intensity distribution in the 3D view.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    ShowIntensityDistribution = property(fget = __GetShowIntensityDistribution, fset = __SetShowIntensityDistribution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the white point type of the standard illuminant.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The ColorSpace property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - D65. Uses a standard daylight illuminant that provides accurate color perception and evaluation.<br>
    #  1 - D50. Uses a natural, horizon light.<br>
    #  2 - C. Uses an average daylight illuminant.<br>
    #  3 - E. Uses an illuminant that gives equal weight to all wavelengths.<br>
    #  4 - User defined. Edits the Color Coordinates of the white point.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    WhitePointType = property(fget = __GetWhitePointType, fset = __SetWhitePointType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the X coordinate of the white point.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The WhitePoint property must be 4.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br> 
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.31271.
    WhitePointX = property(fget = __GetWhitePointX, fset = __SetWhitePointX)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Y coordinate of the white point.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The WhitePoint property must be 4.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.32902.
    WhitePointY = property(fget = __GetWhitePointY, fset = __SetWhitePointY)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the X direction.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  The XDirection property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    #  You can modify the property if the distribution is Asymmetric Gaussian or Library<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    XDirection = property(fget = __GetXDirection, fset = __SetXDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to reverse the X direction.
    # @details 
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the X direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the X direction.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    XDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetXDirectionReversed, fset = __SetXDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the sensor X end dimension value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 50.0 mm.
    XEnd = property(fget = __GetXEnd, fset = __SetXEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the sensor X dimension mirrored value.
    # @details
    #  True: XStart == -XEnd, you can only change the XEnd value.<br>
    #  False: XStart and XEnd can have different value.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    XMirroredExtent = property(fget = __GetXMirroredExtent, fset = __SetXMirroredExtent)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the sensor X start dimension value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is -50.0 mm.
    XStart = property(fget = __GetXStart, fset = __SetXStart)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Y direction.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  The YDirection property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    #  You can modify the property if the distribution is Asymmetric Gaussian or Library<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    YDirection = property(fget = __GetYDirection, fset = __SetYDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to reverse the Y direction.
    # @details
    #  <p>Prerequisite</b>: The IntensityType property must be 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the Y direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the Y direction.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    YDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetYDirectionReversed, fset = __SetYDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the sensor Y start dimension value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 50.0 mm.
    YEnd = property(fget = __GetYEnd, fset = __SetYEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the sensor Y dimension mirrored  value.
    # @details
    #  True: YStart == -YEnd, you can only change the YEnd value.<br>
    #  False: YStart and YEnd can have different value.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    YMirroredExtent = property(fget = __GetYMirroredExtent, fset = __SetYMirroredExtent)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the sensor Y start dimension value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is -50.0 mm.
    YStart = property(fget = __GetYStart, fset = __SetYStart)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceDisplayBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None
SourceDisplayBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SourceDisplayBuilder_swigregister
SourceDisplayBuilder_swigregister(SourceDisplayBuilder)

class SourceLuminaireBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents the builder for a luminaire source.
    @details
     The luminaire source builder is used to create and edit luminaire source features.


     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSourceLuminaireBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SourceLuminaireBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SourceLuminaireBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetAxisSystem(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetAxisSystem(self)

    def __GetIntensityFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetIntensityFilePath(self)

    def __SetIntensityFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___SetIntensityFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetFlux(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetFlux(self)

    def __SetFlux(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___SetFlux(self, value)

    def __GetFluxUnit(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetFluxUnit(self)

    def __SetFluxUnit(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___SetFluxUnit(self, value)

    def __GetFluxFromFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetFluxFromFile(self)

    def __SetFluxFromFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___SetFluxFromFile(self, value)

    def __GetSpectrum(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetSpectrum(self)

    def __SetSpectrum(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___SetSpectrum(self, value)

    def __GetTemperature(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetTemperature(self)

    def __SetTemperature(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___SetTemperature(self, value)

    def __GetSpectrumFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetSpectrumFilePath(self)

    def __SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetNumberOfRays(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetNumberOfRays(self)

    def __SetNumberOfRays(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___SetNumberOfRays(self, value)

    def __GetRayLength(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetRayLength(self)

    def __SetRayLength(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___SetRayLength(self, value)

    def __GetShowIntensityDistribution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___GetShowIntensityDistribution(self)

    def __SetShowIntensityDistribution(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder___SetShowIntensityDistribution(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets the axis system.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: AxisSystem object.
    AxisSystem = property(fget = __GetAxisSystem)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the flux.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsFluxFromFile property must be False.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in lm or W).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.
    # 
    #  The default value is 683.0.
    Flux = property(fget = __GetFlux, fset = __SetFlux)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable or disable getting the flux from file.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables getting the flux from file.<br>
    #  False: Disables getting the flux from file.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    FluxFromFile = property(fget = __GetFluxFromFile, fset = __SetFluxFromFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the flux unit.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IsFluxFromFile property must be False or The IntensityFile property must be set.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Lumen.<br>
    #  1 - Watt.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer. <br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    FluxUnit = property(fget = __GetFluxUnit, fset = __SetFluxUnit)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the intensity distribution file path.
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    IntensityFilePath = property(fget = __GetIntensityFilePath, fset = __SetIntensityFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the number of rays.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    NumberOfRays = property(fget = __GetNumberOfRays, fset = __SetNumberOfRays)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ray length.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 75.0 mm.
    RayLength = property(fget = __GetRayLength, fset = __SetRayLength)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to show the intensity distribution in the 3D view.
    # @details
    #  True: Shows the intensity distribution in the 3D view.<br>
    #  False: Does not show the intensity distribution in the 3D view.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    ShowIntensityDistribution = property(fget = __GetShowIntensityDistribution, fset = __SetShowIntensityDistribution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the spectrum type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Blackbody, with this value the Temperature property is available.<br>
    #  1 - Library, with this value the File property is available.<br>
    #  2 - Incandescent.<br>
    #  3 - Warmwhite fluorescent.<br>
    #  4 - Daylight fluorescent.<br>
    #  5 - White LED.<br>
    #  6 - Halogen.<br>
    #  7 - Metal halide.<br>
    #  8 - High pressure sodium. <br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    Spectrum = property(fget = __GetSpectrum, fset = __SetSpectrum)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the spectrum file path.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The spectrum type must be 1.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    SpectrumFilePath = property(fget = __GetSpectrumFilePath, fset = __SetSpectrumFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the spectrum temperature.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The spectrum type must be 0.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in Kelvin).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 2856.0 Kelvin.
    Temperature = property(fget = __GetTemperature, fset = __SetTemperature)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceLuminaireBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None
SourceLuminaireBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SourceLuminaireBuilder_swigregister
SourceLuminaireBuilder_swigregister(SourceLuminaireBuilder)

class SourceRayFileBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents the builder for a ray file source.
    @details
     The ray file source builder is used to create and edit ray file source features.


     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSourceRayFileBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SourceRayFileBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SourceRayFileBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetAxisSystem(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetAxisSystem(self)

    def __GetRayFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetRayFilePath(self)

    def __SetRayFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetRayFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetFlux(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetFlux(self)

    def __SetFlux(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetFlux(self, value)

    def __GetFluxFromFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetFluxFromFile(self)

    def __SetFluxFromFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetFluxFromFile(self, value)

    def __GetFluxUnit(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetFluxUnit(self)

    def __SetFluxUnit(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetFluxUnit(self, value)

    def __GetSpectrum(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetSpectrum(self)

    def __SetSpectrum(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetSpectrum(self, value)

    def __GetWavelength(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetWavelength(self)

    def __SetWavelength(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetWavelength(self, value)

    def __GetTemperature(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetTemperature(self)

    def __SetTemperature(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetTemperature(self, value)

    def __GetSpectrumFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetSpectrumFilePath(self)

    def __SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetExitGeometries(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetExitGeometries(self)

    def __SetExitGeometries(self, tags):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetExitGeometries(self, tags)

    def __GetNumberOfRays(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetNumberOfRays(self)

    def __SetNumberOfRays(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetNumberOfRays(self, value)

    def __GetRayLength(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___GetRayLength(self)

    def __SetRayLength(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder___SetRayLength(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets the axis system.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: AxisSystem object.
    AxisSystem = property(fget = __GetAxisSystem)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets exit geometries.
    # @details 
    #  The ExitGeometries property takes a list of feature tag and returns a list of feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: List of integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty list.
    ExitGeometries = property(fget = __GetExitGeometries, fset = __SetExitGeometries)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the flux.
    # @details
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in lumen or watt).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  By default the value comes from the ray file, otherwise value is 683. lumen.
    Flux = property(fget = __GetFlux, fset = __SetFlux)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable fetching the flux from file.
    # @details 
    #  True: Enables fetching the flux from file.<br>
    #  False: Disables fetching the flux from file.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is True.
    FluxFromFile = property(fget = __GetFluxFromFile, fset = __SetFluxFromFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the flux unit.
    # @details 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - lumen (lm).<br>
    #  1 - watt (W).<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer. <br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    FluxUnit = property(fget = __GetFluxUnit, fset = __SetFluxUnit)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the number of rays.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    NumberOfRays = property(fget = __GetNumberOfRays, fset = __SetNumberOfRays)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ray file path.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    RayFilePath = property(fget = __GetRayFilePath, fset = __SetRayFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ray length.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in millimeter).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 75.0 mm.
    RayLength = property(fget = __GetRayLength, fset = __SetRayLength)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the spectrum type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Monochromatic, with this value the wavelength property is available.<br>
    #  1 - Blackbody, with this value the temperature property is available.<br>
    #  2 - Library, with this value the spectrum file property is available.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    Spectrum = property(fget = __GetSpectrum, fset = __SetSpectrum)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the spectrum file path.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType must be 1.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    SpectrumFilePath = property(fget = __GetSpectrumFilePath, fset = __SetSpectrumFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the temperature.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType must be 0.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: double (in Kelvin).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 2856.0 K.
    Temperature = property(fget = __GetTemperature, fset = __SetTemperature)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the wavelength.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in nanometer).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 555.0 nm.
    Wavelength = property(fget = __GetWavelength, fset = __SetWavelength)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceRayFileBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None
SourceRayFileBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SourceRayFileBuilder_swigregister
SourceRayFileBuilder_swigregister(SourceRayFileBuilder)

class SourceSurfaceBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents a Surface Source Builder.
    @details
     The Surface Source Builder creates or edits Surface Source features. <br>

     To create a new instance of this class, use FeatureCollection.CreateSourceSurfaceBuilder.<br>

     With a surface source, you can model the light emission of a source taking into account its physical properties as the flux, the spectrum, the exitance and the intensity. A surface source can be defined with any face in a geometry which emits rays.
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SourceSurfaceBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SourceSurfaceBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceSurfaceBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def __GetFluxUnit(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetFluxUnit(self)

    def __SetFluxUnit(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetFluxUnit(self, value)

    def __GetFlux(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetFlux(self)

    def __SetFlux(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetFlux(self, value)

    def __GetUseFluxFromFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetUseFluxFromFile(self)

    def __SetUseFluxFromFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetUseFluxFromFile(self, value)

    def __GetSpectrum(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetSpectrum(self)

    def __SetSpectrum(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetSpectrum(self, value)

    def __GetWavelength(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetWavelength(self)

    def __SetWavelength(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetWavelength(self, value)

    def __GetTemperature(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetTemperature(self)

    def __SetTemperature(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetTemperature(self, value)

    def __GetSpectrumFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetSpectrumFilePath(self)

    def __SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetExitance(self):

    def __GetSourceSurfaceEmissiveFaces(self):

    def __GetExitanceDistributionDirectionReverse(self):

    def __SetExitanceDistributionDirectionReverse(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetExitanceDistributionDirectionReverse(self, value)

    def __GetExitanceXDirectionReversed(self):

    def __SetExitanceXDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetExitanceXDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetExitanceYDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetExitanceYDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetExitanceYDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetExitanceYDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetExitanceOriginPoint(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetExitanceOriginPoint(self)

    def __SetExitanceOriginPoint(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetExitanceOriginPoint(self, tag)

    def __GetExitanceXDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetExitanceXDirection(self)

    def __SetExitanceXDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetExitanceXDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetExitanceYDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetExitanceYDirection(self)

    def __SetExitanceYDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetExitanceYDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetIntensityType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetIntensityType(self)

    def __SetIntensityType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetIntensityType(self, value)

    def __GetIntensityTotalAngle(self):

    def __SetIntensityN(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetIntensityN(self, value)

    def __GetIntensityFWHMAngle(self):

    def __SetIntensityFWHMAngle(self, value):

    def __GetNumberOfRays(self):

    def __GetShowIntensityDistribution(self):

    def __SetShowIntensityDistribution(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetShowIntensityDistribution(self, value)

    def __GetAssociatedGeometries(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetAssociatedGeometries(self)

    def __SetAssociatedGeometries(self, tags):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetAssociatedGeometries(self, tags)

    def __GetExitGeometries(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetExitGeometries(self)

    def __SetExitGeometries(self, tags):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetExitGeometries(self, tags)

    def __GetIntensityXDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetIntensityXDirection(self)

    def __SetIntensityXDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetIntensityXDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetIntensityYDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetIntensityYDirection(self)

    def __SetIntensityYDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetIntensityYDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetIntensityXDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetIntensityXDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetIntensityXDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetIntensityXDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetIntensityYDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___GetIntensityYDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetIntensityYDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder___SetIntensityYDirectionReversed(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets associated geometries.
    # @details 
    #  The AssociatedGeometries property takes a list of feature tag and returns a list of feature tag.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: List of integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty list.
    AssociatedGeometries = property(fget = __GetAssociatedGeometries, fset = __SetAssociatedGeometries)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the exit geometries.
    # @details 
    #  The ExitGeometries property takes a list of feature tag and returns a list of feature tag.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: List of integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty list.
    ExitGeometries = property(fget = __GetExitGeometries, fset = __SetExitGeometries)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the exitance type.
    # @details 
    #  Exitance of a source describes how each point of a surface emits rays.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Constant, ray energy is constant over surface source face.<br>
    #  1 - Variable, ray energy depends on xmp energy distribution.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    Exitance = property(fget = __GetExitance, fset = __SetExitance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to reverse the exitance distribution
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The ExitanteType property must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the exitance distribution direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the exitance distribution direction.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    ExitanceDistributionDirectionReverse = property(fget = __GetExitanceDistributionDirectionReverse, fset = __SetExitanceDistributionDirectionReverse)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the exitance distribution file.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The ExitanteType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    ExitanceDistributionFilePath = property(fget = __GetExitanceDistributionFilePath, fset = __SetExitanceDistributionFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the exitance origin Point
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The ExitanceType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  The ExitanceOriginPoint property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ExitanceOriginPoint = property(fget = __GetExitanceOriginPoint, fset = __SetExitanceOriginPoint)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the exitance X direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The ExitanteType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  The ExitanceXDirection property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ExitanceXDirection = property(fget = __GetExitanceXDirection, fset = __SetExitanceXDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to reverse the exitance of X direction.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The ExitanceType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the exitance direction X.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the exitance direction X.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    ExitanceXDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetExitanceXDirectionReversed, fset = __SetExitanceXDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the exitance Y direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The ExitanteType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  The ExitanceYDirection property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ExitanceYDirection = property(fget = __GetExitanceYDirection, fset = __SetExitanceYDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to reverse the exitance of Y direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The ExitanceType property must be 1.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Reverses the exitance direction Y.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the exitance direction Y.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    ExitanceYDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetExitanceYDirectionReversed, fset = __SetExitanceYDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the flux.
    # @details
    #  The unit depends on the FluxUnitType.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in lm, W or cd).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 683.0 lm for FluxUnitType = 0, 1.0 W for FluxUnitType = 1 and 5.0 cd for FluxUnitType = 2.
    Flux = property(fget = __GetFlux, fset = __SetFlux)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the flux unit type.
    # @details 
    #  The values are: <br>
    #  0 - Lumen.<br>
    #  1 - Watt.<br>
    #  2 - Candela.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</br>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    FluxUnit = property(fget = __GetFluxUnit, fset = __SetFluxUnit)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the distribution file.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnumIntensityType property must be 4.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    IntensityDistributionFilePath = property(fget = __GetIntensityDistributionFilePath, fset = __SetIntensityDistributionFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Full Width At Half Maximum (FWHM) angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnumIntensityType property must be 2.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0, 180].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 30.0 degrees.
    IntensityFWHMAngle = property(fget = __GetIntensityFWHMAngle, fset = __SetIntensityFWHMAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Full Width At Half Maximum (FWHM) X angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnumIntensityType property must be 3.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0, 180].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 30.0 degrees.
    IntensityFWHMAngleX = property(fget = __GetIntensityFWHMAngleX, fset = __SetIntensityFWHMAngleX)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Full Width At Half Maximum (FWHM) Y angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnumIntensityType property must be 3.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0, 180].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 30.0 degrees.
    IntensityFWHMAngleY = property(fget = __GetIntensityFWHMAngleY, fset = __SetIntensityFWHMAngleY)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the N.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnumIntensityType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to -1.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 3.0.
    IntensityN = property(fget = __GetIntensityN, fset = __SetIntensityN)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the orientation type.
    # @details 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - AxisSystem.<br>
    #  1 - NormalToSurface.<br>
    #  2 - NormalToUVMap.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    IntensityOrientation = property(fget = __GetIntensityOrientation, fset = __SetIntensityOrientation)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the intensity total angle.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnumIntensityType property must be 0, 1, 2 or 3.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: [0, 180].<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 180.0 degrees.
    IntensityTotalAngle = property(fget = __GetIntensityTotalAngle, fset = __SetIntensityTotalAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the intensity type of the light source.
    # @details 
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Lambertian.<br>
    #  1 - Cos.<br>
    #  2 - Symmetric Gaussian.<br>
    #  3 - Asymmetric Gaussian.<br>
    #  4 - Library.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    IntensityType = property(fget = __GetIntensityType, fset = __SetIntensityType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the intensity X Direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnumIntensityType property must be 3.<br>
    # 
    #  The property IntensityXDirection takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    IntensityXDirection = property(fget = __GetIntensityXDirection, fset = __SetIntensityXDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to reverse the intensity X direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnumIntensityType property must be 3.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Reverses the intensity X direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the intensity X direction.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    IntensityXDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetIntensityXDirectionReversed, fset = __SetIntensityXDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the intensity Y Direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnumIntensityType property must be 3.<br>
    # 
    #  The property IntensityYDirection takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    IntensityYDirection = property(fget = __GetIntensityYDirection, fset = __SetIntensityYDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to reverse the intensity Y direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnumIntensityType property must be 3 or The IntensityOrientationType must be 0.<br>
    # 
    #  True: Reverses the intensity Y direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the intensity Y direction.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    IntensityYDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetIntensityYDirectionReversed, fset = __SetIntensityYDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the number of rays.
    # @details Edits the value to set the number of rays displayed in the preview.
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    NumberOfRays = property(fget = __GetNumberOfRays, fset = __SetNumberOfRays)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ray length.
    # @details 
    #  Edits the value to set the length of the rays preview in the 3D view.
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 75.0 mm.
    RayLength = property(fget = __GetRayLength, fset = __SetRayLength)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to show the intensity distribution.
    # @details
    #  True: Shows the intensity distribution in the preview.<br>
    #  False: Does not show the intensity distribution in the preview.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    ShowIntensityDistribution = property(fget = __GetShowIntensityDistribution, fset = __SetShowIntensityDistribution)
    ##
    # @brief Returns the interface to edit the emissive faces of the source.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The ExitanteType property must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: SourceSurfaceEmissiveFaces object.
    SourceSurfaceEmissiveFaces = property(fget = __GetSourceSurfaceEmissiveFaces)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the spectrum type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Monochromatic, you can edit the wavelength value.<br>
    #  1 - Blackbody, you can edit the temperature value.<br>
    #  2 - Library, you can browse a .spectrum file.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    Spectrum = property(fget = __GetSpectrum, fset = __SetSpectrum)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the spectrum file.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    SpectrumFilePath = property(fget = __GetSpectrumFilePath, fset = __SetSpectrumFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the temperature.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in Kelvin).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 2856.0 Kelvin.
    Temperature = property(fget = __GetTemperature, fset = __SetTemperature)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to use the flux from file.
    # @details
    #  True: Uses the flux from a file.<br>
    #  False: Does not use the flux from a file.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    UseFluxFromFile = property(fget = __GetUseFluxFromFile, fset = __SetUseFluxFromFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the wavelength.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType property must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in nm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 555.0 nm.
    Wavelength = property(fget = __GetWavelength, fset = __SetWavelength)

SourceSurfaceBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SourceSurfaceBuilder_swigregister
SourceSurfaceBuilder_swigregister(SourceSurfaceBuilder)

class SpeosPatternBuilder(FeatureBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents a Speos pattern builder.
    @details
     The Speos pattern builder is used to create and edit Speos pattern features.<br>

     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSpeosPatternBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SpeosPatternBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [FeatureBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SpeosPatternBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SpeosPatternBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def __GetPatternFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetPatternFilePath(self)

    def __SetPatternFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetPatternFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetOneLayerPerSource(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetOneLayerPerSource(self)

    def __SetOneLayerPerSource(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetOneLayerPerSource(self, value)

    def __GetOrigins(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetOrigins(self)

    def __SetOrigins(self, tags):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetOrigins(self, tags)

    def __GetPreviewMode(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetPreviewMode(self)

    def __SetPreviewMode(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetPreviewMode(self, value)

    def __GetOneLayerPerInstance(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetOneLayerPerInstance(self)

    def __SetOneLayerPerInstance(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetOneLayerPerInstance(self, value)

    def __GetPatternFilePassword(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetPatternFilePassword(self)

    def __SetPatternFilePassword(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetPatternFilePassword(self, value)

    def __GetRayFileFlux(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetRayFileFlux(self)

    def __SetRayFileFlux(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetRayFileFlux(self, value)

    def __GetRayFileFluxUnit(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetRayFileFluxUnit(self)

    def __SetRayFileFluxUnit(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetRayFileFluxUnit(self, value)

    def __GetRayFileFluxFromFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetRayFileFluxFromFile(self)

    def __SetRayFileFluxFromFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetRayFileFluxFromFile(self, value)

    def __GetRayFileSpectrumType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetRayFileSpectrumType(self)

    def __SetRayFileSpectrumType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetRayFileSpectrumType(self, value)

    def __GetRayFileWavelength(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetRayFileWavelength(self)

    def __SetRayFileWavelength(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetRayFileWavelength(self, value)

    def __GetRayFileTemperature(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetRayFileTemperature(self)

    def __SetRayFileTemperature(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetRayFileTemperature(self, value)

    def __GetSpectrumFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetSpectrumFilePath(self)

    def __SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetNumberOfRay(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetNumberOfRay(self)

    def __SetNumberOfRay(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetNumberOfRay(self, value)

    def __GetRayLength(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetRayLength(self)

    def __SetRayLength(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___SetRayLength(self, value)

    def __GetRayFileData(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder___GetRayFileData(self)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the number of rays.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior or equal to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    NumberOfRay = property(fget = __GetNumberOfRay, fset = __SetNumberOfRay)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable/disable one layer per instance.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables one layer per instance.<br>
    #  False: Disables one layer per instance.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Pattern file must be a Lightbox file.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    OneLayerPerInstance = property(fget = __GetOneLayerPerInstance, fset = __SetOneLayerPerInstance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable/disable one layer per source.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables one layer per source.<br>
    #  False: Disables one layer per source.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    OneLayerPerSource = property(fget = __GetOneLayerPerSource, fset = __SetOneLayerPerSource)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the origin coordinate systems.
    # @details
    #  This property takes/returns a list of NX Datum System feature tags.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: List of integer (NX Tags).<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty list.
    Origins = property(fget = __GetOrigins, fset = __SetOrigins)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the pattern file password.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Pattern file must be a Lightbox file.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    PatternFilePassword = property(fget = __GetPatternFilePassword, fset = __SetPatternFilePassword)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property pattern file path.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty file path (string).
    PatternFilePath = property(fget = __GetPatternFilePath, fset = __SetPatternFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the preview mode.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Meshing.<br>
    #  1 - BoundingBox.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is Meshing (0).
    PreviewMode = property(fget = __GetPreviewMode, fset = __SetPreviewMode)
    ##
    # @brief Returns the ray file data object.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: CRayFileData.<br>
    #  This object allows to read data from a ray file.<br>
    RayFileData = property(fget = __GetRayFileData)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the flux of the ray file source.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Pattern file must be a ray file.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in lumen or watt).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  By default the value comes from the ray file, otherwise value is 683. lumen.
    RayFileFlux = property(fget = __GetRayFileFlux, fset = __SetRayFileFlux)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable fetching the flux from file.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables fetching the flux from file.<br>
    #  False: Disables fetching the flux from file.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    RayFileFluxFromFile = property(fget = __GetRayFileFluxFromFile, fset = __SetRayFileFluxFromFile)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the flux unit of the ray file source.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Pattern file must be a ray file.<br>
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - lumen (lm).<br>
    #  1 - watt (W).<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer. <br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    RayFileFluxUnit = property(fget = __GetRayFileFluxUnit, fset = __SetRayFileFluxUnit)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the spectrum type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Monochromatic, with this value the wavelength property is available.<br>
    #  1 - Blackbody, with this value the temperature property is available.<br>
    #  2 - Library, with this value the spectrum file property is available.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    RayFileSpectrumType = property(fget = __GetRayFileSpectrumType, fset = __SetRayFileSpectrumType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the temperature.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType must be 0.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: double (in Kelvin).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 2856.0 K.
    RayFileTemperature = property(fget = __GetRayFileTemperature, fset = __SetRayFileTemperature)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the wavelength.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in nanometer).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 555.0 nm.
    RayFileWavelength = property(fget = __GetRayFileWavelength, fset = __SetRayFileWavelength)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ray length.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in millimeter).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 75.0 mm.
    RayLength = property(fget = __GetRayLength, fset = __SetRayLength)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the spectrum file path.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType must be 1.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    SpectrumFilePath = property(fget = __GetSpectrumFilePath, fset = __SetSpectrumFilePath)

SpeosPatternBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SpeosPatternBuilder_swigregister
SpeosPatternBuilder_swigregister(SpeosPatternBuilder)

class FeatureSimulation(Feature):
    """
    @brief Represents a Speos simulation feature.
    @details
     A base class for all Speos simulation features.<br>

     This is an abstract class that provides the basic functionality common to all simulation features.<br>
     This is an abstract class, and cannot be instantiated.<br>
     To obtain an instance of this class, refer to the simulation builders.<br>
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [Feature]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, FeatureSimulation, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [Feature]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, FeatureSimulation, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_FeatureSimulation
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def Isolate(self):
        """
        @brief Isolates the simulation and its results.
        @details 
         <b>Prerequisite</b>: The simulation must be updated.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureSimulation_Isolate(self)


    def Export(self, path):
        """
        @brief Exports the simulation to a specified location.
        @details
         <b>Prerequisite</b>: The simulation must be updated.
        @param[in] path : The output folder.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureSimulation_Export(self, path)


    def LinkedExport(self):
        """
        @brief Exports the simulation to the Speos isolated folder.
        @details 
         Exports the simulation to the folder "./Speos isolated folder/"
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureSimulation_LinkedExport(self)


    def RegenerationSpeosHPC(self):
        """
        @brief Runs the simulation on the Speos HPC cluster.
        @details 
         <b>Prerequisite</b>: The Speos HPC cluster must be configured.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureSimulation_RegenerationSpeosHPC(self)


    def __SetGPUSimulationMode(self, ibGPUSimulationMode):
        return _SpeosNX.FeatureSimulation___SetGPUSimulationMode(self, ibGPUSimulationMode)

    ##
    # @brief Sets the simulation mode.
    # @details
    #  True: GPU simulation.<br>
    #  False: CPU simulation.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    GPUSimulationMode = property(fset = __SetGPUSimulationMode)

FeatureSimulation_swigregister = _SpeosNX.FeatureSimulation_swigregister
FeatureSimulation_swigregister(FeatureSimulation)

class Part(_object):
    """@brief Represents a Speos For NX part."""

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, Part, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, Part, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_Part
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def __GetFeatures(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Part___GetFeatures(self)

    def __GetName(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Part___GetName(self)

    ##
    # @brief Returns the @link FeatureCollection @endlink instance belonging to this part.
    # @return The @link FeatureCollection @endlink.
    Features = property(fget = __GetFeatures)
    Name = property(fget = __GetName)

Part_swigregister = _SpeosNX.Part_swigregister
Part_swigregister(Part)

class SensorIntensityBuilder(SensorCommonBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents an Intensity Sensor Builder.
    @details
     The Intensity Sensor Builder is used to create and edit Intensity Sensor features.

     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSensorIntensityBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [SensorCommonBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SensorIntensityBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [SensorCommonBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SensorIntensityBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
