        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetOrientation(self, value)

    def __GetAdaptiveSampling(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetAdaptiveSampling(self)

    def __SetAdaptiveSampling(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetAdaptiveSampling(self, value)

    def __GetPolarFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetPolarFilePath(self)

    def __SetPolarFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetPolarFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetConoscopicThetaMax(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetConoscopicThetaMax(self)

    def __SetConoscopicThetaMax(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetConoscopicThetaMax(self, value)

    def __GetConoscopicSampling(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetConoscopicSampling(self)

    def __SetConoscopicSampling(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetConoscopicSampling(self, value)

    def __GetConoscopicResolution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetConoscopicResolution(self)

    def __SetConoscopicResolution(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetConoscopicResolution(self, value)

    def __GetPolarXStart(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetPolarXStart(self)

    def __GetPolarXEnd(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetPolarXEnd(self)

    def __GetPolarXSampling(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetPolarXSampling(self)

    def __SetPolarXSampling(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetPolarXSampling(self, value)

    def __GetPolarXResolution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetPolarXResolution(self)

    def __SetPolarXResolution(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetPolarXResolution(self, value)

    def __GetPolarYStart(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetPolarYStart(self)

    def __GetPolarYEnd(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetPolarYEnd(self)

    def __GetPolarYSampling(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetPolarYSampling(self)

    def __SetPolarYSampling(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetPolarYSampling(self, value)

    def __GetPolarYResolution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetPolarYResolution(self)

    def __SetPolarYResolution(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetPolarYResolution(self, value)

    def __GetNearField(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetNearField(self)

    def __SetNearField(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetNearField(self, value)

    def __GetCellDistance(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetCellDistance(self)

    def __SetCellDistance(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetCellDistance(self, value)

    def __GetCellDiameter(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetCellDiameter(self)

    def __SetCellDiameter(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetCellDiameter(self, value)

    def __GetIntensityResultViewingDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetIntensityResultViewingDirection(self)

    def __SetIntensityResultViewingDirection(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetIntensityResultViewingDirection(self, value)

    def __GetIntegrationAngle(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetIntegrationAngle(self)

    def __SetIntegrationAngle(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetIntegrationAngle(self, value)

    def __GetRadius(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___GetRadius(self)

    def __SetRadius(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder___SetRadius(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable adaptive sampling.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The FormatType property must be 1, 2, 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Activates adaptive Sampling.<br>
    #  False: Deactivates adaptive Sampling.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    AdaptiveSampling = property(fget = __GetAdaptiveSampling, fset = __SetAdaptiveSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the cell diameter.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnableNearField property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 174.9773 mm.
    CellDiameter = property(fget = __GetCellDiameter, fset = __SetCellDiameter)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the cell distance.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnableNearField property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 1000.0 mm.
    CellDistance = property(fget = __GetCellDistance, fset = __SetCellDistance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Conoscopic resolution.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The OrientationType property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    ConoscopicResolution = property(fget = __GetConoscopicResolution, fset = __SetConoscopicResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Conoscopic sampling. 
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The OrientationType property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 90.
    ConoscopicSampling = property(fget = __GetConoscopicSampling, fset = __SetConoscopicSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Conoscopic theta maximum value.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The OrientationType property must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 90.0.
    ConoscopicThetaMax = property(fget = __GetConoscopicThetaMax, fset = __SetConoscopicThetaMax)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the format type.
    # @details 
    #  These formats correspond to light distribution standards and will generate different file formats as an output.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - XMP<br>
    #  1 - IESNA Type A.<br>
    #  2 - IESNA Type B.<br>
    #  3 - IESNA Type C.<br>
    #  4 - Eulumdat.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    Format = property(fget = __GetFormat, fset = __SetFormat)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the integration angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The OrientationType property must be 1, 2, 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  This parameter appears only for IESNA and Eulumdat formats.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: (0.0, 90.0)<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 5.0 degrees.
    IntegrationAngle = property(fget = __GetIntegrationAngle, fset = __SetIntegrationAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the intensity result viewing direction.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The OrientationType property must be 0 or 1.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - From source looking at sensor, The viewing direction of the observer is the same as the light direction emitted.<br>
    #  1 - From sensor looking at source, The viewing direction of the observer is in the opposite of the light direction.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    IntensityResultViewingDirection = property(fget = __GetIntensityResultViewingDirection, fset = __SetIntensityResultViewingDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable near-field.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables Near Field.<br>
    #  False: Disables Near Field.<br>
    #  
    #   <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    NearField = property(fget = __GetNearField, fset = __SetNearField)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the orientation type.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The FormatType property must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - X as Parallel, Y as Meridian, for a polar parameterization with the poles along the X axis.<br>
    #  1 - X as Meridian, Y as Parallel, for a polar parameterization with the poles along the Y axis.<br>
    #  2 - Conoscopic, for a polar parameterization with the poles along the Z axis.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    Orientation = property(fget = __GetOrientation, fset = __SetOrientation)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the polar file path.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnableAdaptiveSampling property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    PolarFilePath = property(fget = __GetPolarFilePath, fset = __SetPolarFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the polar X end.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The FormatType property must be 1, 2, 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    PolarXEnd = property(fget = __GetPolarXEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the polar X resolution.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The FormatType property must be 1, 2, 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    PolarXResolution = property(fget = __GetPolarXResolution, fset = __SetPolarXResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the polar X sampling.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The FormatType property must be 1, 2, 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value are: <br>
    #  37 for IESNA Type A and IESNA Type B.<br>
    #  36 for IESNA Type C and Eulumdat.
    PolarXSampling = property(fget = __GetPolarXSampling, fset = __SetPolarXSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the polar X start.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The FormatType property must be 1, 2, 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    PolarXStart = property(fget = __GetPolarXStart)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the polar Y end.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The FormatType property must be 1, 2, 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    PolarYEnd = property(fget = __GetPolarYEnd)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the polar Y resolution.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The FormatType property must be 1, 2, 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    PolarYResolution = property(fget = __GetPolarYResolution, fset = __SetPolarYResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the polar Y sampling.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The FormatType property must be 1, 2, 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value are: <br>
    #  37 for IESNA Type A and IESNA Type B.<br>
    #  19 for IESNA Type C and Eulumdat.
    PolarYSampling = property(fget = __GetPolarYSampling, fset = __SetPolarYSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the polar Y start.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The FormatType property must be 1, 2, 3 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    PolarYStart = property(fget = __GetPolarYStart)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the radius.
    # @details 
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The parameter must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 1000.0 mm.
    Radius = property(fget = __GetRadius, fset = __SetRadius)

SensorIntensityBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SensorIntensityBuilder_swigregister
SensorIntensityBuilder_swigregister(SensorIntensityBuilder)

class SensorIrradianceBuilder(SensorCommonBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents an Irradiance Sensor Builder.
    @details
     The Irradiance Sensor Builder is used to create and edit Irradiance Sensor features.

     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSensorIrradianceBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [SensorCommonBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SensorIrradianceBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [SensorCommonBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SensorIrradianceBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SensorIrradianceBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def __GetUseRayFile(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___GetUseRayFile(self)

    def __SetUseRayFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___SetUseRayFile(self, value)

    def __GetRayFileFormat(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___GetRayFileFormat(self)

    def __SetRayFileFormat(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___SetRayFileFormat(self, value)

    def __GetIntegrationType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___GetIntegrationType(self)

    def __SetIntegrationType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___SetIntegrationType(self, value)

    def __GetIntegrationDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___GetIntegrationDirection(self)

    def __SetIntegrationDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___SetIntegrationDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetIntegrationDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___GetIntegrationDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetIntegrationDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___SetIntegrationDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetOutputFaces(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___GetOutputFaces(self)

    def __SetOutputFaces(self, objects):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder___SetOutputFaces(self, objects)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the integration direction.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IntegrationType property must be 0, 2 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  The integration direction property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    IntegrationDirection = property(fget = __GetIntegrationDirection, fset = __SetIntegrationDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the reverse direction of integration.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The IntegrationType property must be 0, 2 or 4.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the IntegrationDirection property<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the IntegrationDirection property<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    IntegrationDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetIntegrationDirectionReversed, fset = __SetIntegrationDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the integration type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Planar.<br>
    #  1 - Radial.<br>
    #  2 - Hemishperical.<br>
    #  3 - Cylindrical.<br>
    #  4 - Semi-cylindrical.
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    IntegrationType = property(fget = __GetIntegrationType, fset = __SetIntegrationType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the output faces.
    # @details 
    #  The output faces property takes a list of feature tag and returns a list of feature tag.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: List of integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty list.
    OutputFaces = property(fget = __GetOutputFaces, fset = __SetOutputFaces)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ray file format.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnableRayFile property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  Defines the type of ray file.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Speos without Polarization.<br>
    #  1 - Speos with Polarization.<br>
    #  2 - IES TM-25 without Polarization.<br>
    #  3 - IES TM-25 with Polarization.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    RayFileFormat = property(fget = __GetRayFileFormat, fset = __SetRayFileFormat)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable ray file.
    # @details 
    #  True: Enables Ray file.<br>
    #  False: Disables Ray file.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    UseRayFile = property(fget = __GetUseRayFile, fset = __SetUseRayFile)

SensorIrradianceBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SensorIrradianceBuilder_swigregister
SensorIrradianceBuilder_swigregister(SensorIrradianceBuilder)

    """

    """

        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetFocal(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetFocal(self)

    def __SetFocal(self, value):

    def __GetFrameObserverPoint(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetFrameObserverPoint(self)

    def __SetFrameObserverPoint(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetFrameObserverPoint(self, tag)

    def __GetIntegrationAngle(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetIntegrationAngle(self)

    def __SetIntegrationAngle(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetIntegrationAngle(self, value)

    def __GetObserverPoint(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverPoint(self)

    def __SetObserverPoint(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetObserverPoint(self, tag)

    def __GetObserverFrontDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverFrontDirection(self)

    def __SetObserverFrontDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetObserverFrontDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetObserverTopDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverTopDirection(self)

    def __SetObserverTopDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetObserverTopDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetObserverFrontDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverFrontDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetObserverFrontDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetObserverFrontDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetObserverTopDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverTopDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetObserverTopDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetObserverTopDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetObserverHorizontalFOV(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverHorizontalFOV(self)

    def __SetObserverHorizontalFOV(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetObserverHorizontalFOV(self, value)

    def __GetObserverVerticalFOV(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverVerticalFOV(self)

    def __SetObserverVerticalFOV(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetObserverVerticalFOV(self, value)

    def __GetObserverHorizontalSampling(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverHorizontalSampling(self)

    def __SetObserverHorizontalSampling(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetObserverHorizontalSampling(self, value)

    def __GetObserverVerticalSampling(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverVerticalSampling(self)

    def __SetObserverVerticalSampling(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetObserverVerticalSampling(self, value)

    def __GetObserverHorizontalResolution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverHorizontalResolution(self)

    def __GetObserverVerticalResolution(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetObserverVerticalResolution(self)

    def __GetAutomaticFraming(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___GetAutomaticFraming(self)

    def __SetAutomaticFraming(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder___SetAutomaticFraming(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable automatic framing.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2 or the ObserverType must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  Automatic Framing reframes the camera on the radiance sensor.<br>
    #  
    #  True : Enable Automatic Framing.<br>
    #  False : Disable Automatic Framing.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    AutomaticFraming = property(fget = __GetAutomaticFraming, fset = __SetAutomaticFraming)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the camera by its name.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    CameraName = property(fget = __GetCameraName, fset = __SetCameraName)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the definition type.
    # @details 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Frame.<br>
    #  1 - Camera.<br>
    #  2 - Observer.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    Definition = property(fget = __GetDefinition, fset = __SetDefinition)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the focal.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType property must be 2 or the ObserverType must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  Focal defines the distance between the sensor plane and the Observer point.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in mm).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 250.0 mm.
    Focal = property(fget = __GetFocal, fset = __SetFocal)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the frame observer point.
    # @details      
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The ObserverType must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  The property frame observer point takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    #  Defines the location of the frame.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    FrameObserverPoint = property(fget = __GetFrameObserverPoint, fset = __SetFrameObserverPoint)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the H/V ratio.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  H/V Ratio modifies the X Start and X End values according to the Y Start and Y End values.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 1.33.
    HVRatio = property(fget = __GetHVRatio, fset = __SetHVRatio)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the integration angle.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: (0.0, 90.0)<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 5.0 degrees.
    IntegrationAngle = property(fget = __GetIntegrationAngle, fset = __SetIntegrationAngle)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the observer type.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType property must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 : Focal.<br>
    #  1 : Observer.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    Observer = property(fget = __GetObserver, fset = __SetObserver)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the observer front direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  The property observer front direction takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ObserverFrontDirection = property(fget = __GetObserverFrontDirection, fset = __SetObserverFrontDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reverse direction of observer front direction.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the observer front direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the Observer Front Direction.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    ObserverFrontDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetObserverFrontDirectionReversed, fset = __SetObserverFrontDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the observer horizontal field of view.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in degrees).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: (0, 180)<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 2.0 degrees.
    ObserverHorizontalFOV = property(fget = __GetObserverHorizontalFOV, fset = __SetObserverHorizontalFOV)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the observer horizontal resolution.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    ObserverHorizontalResolution = property(fget = __GetObserverHorizontalResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the observer horizontal sampling.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    ObserverHorizontalSampling = property(fget = __GetObserverHorizontalSampling, fset = __SetObserverHorizontalSampling)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the observer point.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  The property observer point takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    #  Defines the location of the observer.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ObserverPoint = property(fget = __GetObserverPoint, fset = __SetObserverPoint)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the observer top direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  The property observer top direction takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ObserverTopDirection = property(fget = __GetObserverTopDirection, fset = __SetObserverTopDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reverse direction of observer top direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the Observer top Direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the observer top direction.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    ObserverTopDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetObserverTopDirectionReversed, fset = __SetObserverTopDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the observer vertical field of view.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: (0, 180)<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 2.0 degrees.
    ObserverVerticalFOV = property(fget = __GetObserverVerticalFOV, fset = __SetObserverVerticalFOV)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the observer vertical resolution.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    ObserverVerticalResolution = property(fget = __GetObserverVerticalResolution)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the observer vertical sampling.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The DefinitionType must be 2.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 100.
    ObserverVerticalSampling = property(fget = __GetObserverVerticalSampling, fset = __SetObserverVerticalSampling)

SensorRadianceBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SensorRadianceBuilder_swigregister
SensorRadianceBuilder_swigregister(SensorRadianceBuilder)

        return _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder___GetUseRayFile(self)

    def __SetUseRayFile(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder___SetUseRayFile(self, value)

    def __GetRayFileFormat(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder___GetRayFileFormat(self)

    def __SetRayFileFormat(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder___SetRayFileFormat(self, value)

    def __GetMaximumNumberOfPaths(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder___GetMaximumNumberOfPaths(self)

    def __SetMaximumNumberOfPaths(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder___SetMaximumNumberOfPaths(self, value)

    def __GetUsePartFamilies(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder___GetUsePartFamilies(self)

    def __SetUsePartFamilies(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder___SetUsePartFamilies(self, value)

    def __GetFamilySelection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder___GetFamilySelection(self)

    def __SetFamilySelection(self, selectionVec):
        return _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder___SetFamilySelection(self, selectionVec)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the duration.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The StopOnDuration property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  Time necessary to reach for the simulation to end. <br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in second).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 1800.0 s.
    Duration = property(fget = __GetDuration, fset = __SetDuration)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the family selection list.
    # @details  
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseFamilyTables property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  Selects the configurations to run with the simulation.
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: List of string.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty list.
    FamilySelection = property(fget = __GetFamilySelection, fset = __SetFamilySelection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the maximum number of paths.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnableLightExpert property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  The Maximum paths corresponds to the maximum number of rays the Light Path Finder file (*.lpf or *.lp3) can contain.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 100,000.
    MaximumNumberOfPaths = property(fget = __GetMaximumNumberOfPaths, fset = __SetMaximumNumberOfPaths)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ray file format.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The EnableRayFile property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  Type of ray file that the simulation creates at the end.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Speos without Polarization.<br>
    #  1 - Speos with Polarization.<br>
    #  2 - IES TM-25 without Polarization.<br>
    #  3 - IES TM-25 with Polarization.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    RayFileFormat = property(fget = __GetRayFileFormat, fset = __SetRayFileFormat)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the ray number multiplier.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The StopOnRaysNumber property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Rays.<br>
    #  1 - Kilo-Rays.<br>
    #  2 - Mega-Rays.<br>
    #  3 - Giga-Rays.
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 1.
    RayNumberMultiplier = property(fget = __GetRayNumberMultiplier, fset = __SetRayNumberMultiplier)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the number or rays.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The StopOnRaysNumber property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  Number of rays necessary to reach for the simulation to end.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 200.
    RaysNumber = property(fget = __GetRaysNumber, fset = __SetRaysNumber)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to stop on duration.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables stop on Duration property<br>
    #  False: Disables stop on Duration property<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    StopOnDuration = property(fget = __GetStopOnDuration, fset = __SetStopOnDuration)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable stop on rays number.
    # @details 
    #  True: Enables stop on RaysNumber property.<br>
    #  False: Disables stop on RaysNumber property.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is True.
    StopOnRaysNumber = property(fget = __GetStopOnRaysNumber, fset = __SetStopOnRaysNumber)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to use family tables.
    # @details 
    #  True: Enables multi-configuration to run in the simulation.<br>
    #  False: Disables multi-configuration to run in the simulation.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    UsePartFamilies = property(fget = __GetUsePartFamilies, fset = __SetUsePartFamilies)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable ray file.
    # @details
    #  True: Enables Ray file.<br>
    #  False: Disables Ray file.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    UseRayFile = property(fget = __GetUseRayFile, fset = __SetUseRayFile)

SimulationDirectBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SimulationDirectBuilder_swigregister
SimulationDirectBuilder_swigregister(SimulationDirectBuilder)

class SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder(SourceAmbientCommonBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents the builder for an Ambient Source with CIE Standard General Sky type.
    @details
     The Ambient General Sky Source Builder is used to create and edit Ambient General Sky Source features.

     This sky model is based on the publication of the CIE: ISO 15469:2004/CIE S 011:2003: Spatial distribution of daylight - CIE standard general sky.

     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [SourceAmbientCommonBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [SourceAmbientCommonBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetZenithNorthSystem(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___GetZenithNorthSystem(self)

    def __GetLuminance(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___GetLuminance(self)

    def __SetLuminance(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___SetLuminance(self, value)

    def __GetCIEType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___GetCIEType(self)

    def __SetCIEType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___SetCIEType(self, value)

    def __GetSunType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___GetSunType(self)

    def __SetSunType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___SetSunType(self, value)

    def __GetSunDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___GetSunDirection(self)

    def __SetSunDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___SetSunDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetSunDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___GetSunDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetSunDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___SetSunDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetTimezone(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder___GetTimezone(self)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the CIE type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - CIE standard overcast sky.<br>
    #  1 - Overcast with steep luminance gradation and slight brightening towards the sun.<br>
    #  2 - Overcast, moderately graded with azimuthal uniformity.<br>
    #  3 - Overcast, moderately graded and slight brightening towards the sun.<br>
    #  4 - Sky of uniform luminance.<br>
    #  5 - Partly cloudy sky, no gradation towards zenith, slight brightnening.<br>
    #  6 - Partly cloudy sky, no gradation towards zenith, brighter circumsolar region.<br>
    #  7 - Partly cloudy sky, no gradation towards zenith, distinct solar corona.<br>
    #  8 - Partly cloudy sky, with the obscured sun.<br>
    #  9 - Partly cloudy sky, with brighter circumsolar region.<br>
    #  10 - White blue sky with distinct solar corona.<br>
    #  11 - CIE standard clear sky, low luminance turbidity. <br>
    #  12 - CIE standard clear sky, polluted atmosphere.<br>
    #  13 - Cloudless turbid sky with broad solar corona.<br>
    #  14 - White blue turbid sky with broad solar corona.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 5.
    CIEType = property(fget = __GetCIEType, fset = __SetCIEType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the luminance
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in cd/m2).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 1000.0 cd/m2.
    Luminance = property(fget = __GetLuminance, fset = __SetLuminance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sun direction.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SunType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  The Sun direction property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    SunDirection = property(fget = __GetSunDirection, fset = __SetSunDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reverse Sun direction.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SunType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the Sun direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the Sun direction.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    SunDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetSunDirectionReversed, fset = __SetSunDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sun type.
    # @details 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Automatic, you must set the values in the Timezone and Location object.<br>
    #  1 - Direction,  you must to set the sun direction property.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    SunType = property(fget = __GetSunType, fset = __SetSunType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the Timezone and Location object.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SunType property must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Timezone object.<br>
    Timezone = property(fget = __GetTimezone)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the orientation object of the source.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: ZenithNorthSystem object.
    ZenithNorthSystem = property(fget = __GetZenithNorthSystem)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None
SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder_swigregister
SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder_swigregister(SourceAmbientGeneralSkyBuilder)

        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder___GetSunDirection(self)

        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder___SetSunDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetSunDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder___GetSunDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetSunDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder___SetSunDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetTurbidity(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder___GetTurbidity(self)

    def __SetTurbidity(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder___SetTurbidity(self, value)

    def __GetWithSky(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder___GetWithSky(self)

    def __SetWithSky(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder___SetWithSky(self, value)

    def __GetTimezone(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder___GetTimezone(self)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sun direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SunType property must be 1.<br> 
    #  
    #  The Sun direction property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    SunDirection = property(fget = __GetSunDirection, fset = __SetSunDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reverse Sun direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SunType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the Sun direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the Sun direction.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    SunDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetSunDirectionReversed, fset = __SetSunDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sun type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Automatic, you must set the values in the Timezone object.<br>
    #  1 - Direction,  you must to set the sun direction property.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    SunType = property(fget = __GetSunType, fset = __SetSunType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the Timezone and Location object.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SunType property must be 0.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Timezone object.<br>
    Timezone = property(fget = __GetTimezone)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the turbidity.
    # @details 
    #  Turbidity is a measure of the fraction of scattering due to haze as opposed to molecules.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double.<br> 
    #  <b>Range</b>: [2.0, 9.0]<br> 
    #  
    #  The default value is 3.0.
    Turbidity = property(fget = __GetTurbidity, fset = __SetTurbidity)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable the sky.
    # @details 
    #  True: Uses the sun and Sky in simulations.<br>
    #  False: Uses sun only in simulations.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is True.
    WithSky = property(fget = __GetWithSky, fset = __SetWithSky)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the orientation object of the source.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: ZenithNorthSystem object.
    ZenithNorthSystem = property(fget = __GetZenithNorthSystem)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None
SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder_swigregister
SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder_swigregister(SourceAmbientNaturalLightBuilder)

class SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder(SourceAmbientCommonBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents the builder for an Ambient Source with CIE Standard Overcast Sky type.
    @details
     The Ambient Overcast Sky Source Builder is used to create and edit Ambient Overcast Sky Source features.

     This sky model is based on the publication of the CIE: ISO 15469:2004/CIE S 011:2003: Spatial distribution of daylight - CIE standard general sky.

     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [SourceAmbientCommonBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [SourceAmbientCommonBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetZenithDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___GetZenithDirection(self)

    def __SetZenithDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___SetZenithDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetZenithDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___GetZenithDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetZenithDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___SetZenithDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetLuminance(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___GetLuminance(self)

    def __SetLuminance(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___SetLuminance(self, value)

    def __GetSpectrum(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___GetSpectrum(self)

    def __SetSpectrum(self, etype):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___SetSpectrum(self, etype)

    def __GetSpectrumFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___GetSpectrumFilePath(self)

    def __SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetTemperature(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___GetTemperature(self)

    def __SetTemperature(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder___SetTemperature(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the luminance
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (cd/m2).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 1000.0 cd/m2.
    Luminance = property(fget = __GetLuminance, fset = __SetLuminance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the spectrum type.
    # @details 
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Blackbody, then in the Temperature property, set the blackbody temperature of the source spectrum in Kelvin.<br>
    #  1 - Library, then in the File property, browse a .spectrum file.
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 0.
    Spectrum = property(fget = __GetSpectrum, fset = __SetSpectrum)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the spectrum file path.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    SpectrumFilePath = property(fget = __GetSpectrumFilePath, fset = __SetSpectrumFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the temperature.
    # @details 
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType property must be 0.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in Kelvin).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is 8000.0 Kelvin.
    Temperature = property(fget = __GetTemperature, fset = __SetTemperature)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the zenith direction.
    # @details
    #  The zenith direction property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ZenithDirection = property(fget = __GetZenithDirection, fset = __SetZenithDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reverse zenith direction.
    # @details
    #  True: Reverses the zenith direction.<br>
    #  False: Not reverse the zenith direction<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    ZenithDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetZenithDirectionReversed, fset = __SetZenithDirectionReversed)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None
SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder_swigregister
SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder_swigregister(SourceAmbientOvercastSkyBuilder)

class SourceAmbientUS1976Builder(SourceAmbientCommonBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents the builder for an U.S Standard Atmosphere 1976 Source.
    @details
     The Ambient US1976 Sky Source Builder is used to create and edit Ambient US1976 Sky Source features.

     The U.S Standard Atmosphere 1976 source allows you to generate light from the sky according to a time and location.
     With this source, signals can be collected outside the visible spectrum including in the infrared.

     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSourceAmbientUS1976Builder @endlink
    """

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [SourceAmbientCommonBuilder]:
        __swig_setmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_setmethods__', {}))
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, SourceAmbientUS1976Builder, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    for _s in [SourceAmbientCommonBuilder]:
        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SourceAmbientUS1976Builder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

    def __GetZenithNorthSystem(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUS1976Builder___GetZenithNorthSystem(self)

    def __GetSunType(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUS1976Builder___GetSunType(self)

    def __SetSunType(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUS1976Builder___SetSunType(self, value)

    def __GetSunDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUS1976Builder___GetSunDirection(self)

    def __SetSunDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUS1976Builder___SetSunDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetSunDirectionReversed(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUS1976Builder___GetSunDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetSunDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUS1976Builder___SetSunDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetTimezone(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUS1976Builder___GetTimezone(self)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sun direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SunType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  The Sun direction property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    SunDirection = property(fget = __GetSunDirection, fset = __SetSunDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reverse Sun direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SunType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the Sun direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the Sun direction.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    SunDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetSunDirectionReversed, fset = __SetSunDirectionReversed)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sun type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0 - Automatic, you must set the values in the Timezone object.<br>
    #  1 - Direction,  you must to set the sun direction property.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    SunType = property(fget = __GetSunType, fset = __SetSunType)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the Timezone and Location object.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SunType property must be 0.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Timezone object.<br>
    Timezone = property(fget = __GetTimezone)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the orientation object of the source.
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: ZenithNorthSystem object.
    ZenithNorthSystem = property(fget = __GetZenithNorthSystem)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceAmbientUS1976Builder
    __del__ = lambda self: None
SourceAmbientUS1976Builder_swigregister = _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUS1976Builder_swigregister
SourceAmbientUS1976Builder_swigregister(SourceAmbientUS1976Builder)

class SourceAmbientUniformBuilder(SourceAmbientCommonBuilder):
    """
    @brief Represents the builder for an Ambient Source with Uniform type.
    @details
     The Ambient Uniform Source Builder is used to create and edit Ambient Uniform Source features.

     To create a new instance of this class, use @link FeatureCollection::CreateSourceAmbientUniformBuilder @endlink
    """

    for _s in [SourceAmbientCommonBuilder]:

        __swig_getmethods__.update(getattr(_s, '__swig_getmethods__', {}))
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, SourceAmbientUniformBuilder, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr

        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___GetZenithDirectionReversed(self)

    def __SetZenithDirectionReversed(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___SetZenithDirectionReversed(self, value)

    def __GetLuminance(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___GetLuminance(self)

    def __SetLuminance(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___SetLuminance(self, value)

    def __GetSpectrum(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___GetSpectrum(self)

    def __SetSpectrum(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___SetSpectrum(self, value)

    def __GetSpectrumFilePath(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___GetSpectrumFilePath(self)

    def __SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___SetSpectrumFilePath(self, value)

    def __GetTemperature(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___GetTemperature(self)

    def __SetTemperature(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___SetTemperature(self, value)

    def __GetMirroredExtent(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___GetMirroredExtent(self)

    def __SetMirroredExtent(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___SetMirroredExtent(self, value)

    def __GetSun(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___GetSun(self)

    def __SetSun(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___SetSun(self, value)

    def __GetSunDirection(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___GetSunDirection(self)

    def __SetSunDirection(self, tag):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___SetSunDirection(self, tag)

    def __GetSunDirectionReverse(self):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___GetSunDirectionReverse(self)

    def __SetSunDirectionReverse(self, value):
        return _SpeosNX.SourceAmbientUniformBuilder___SetSunDirectionReverse(self, value)

    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the luminance
    # @details
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Double (in cd/m2).<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 1000.0 cd/m2.
    Luminance = property(fget = __GetLuminance, fset = __SetLuminance)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable mirrored extent.
    # @details 
    #  True: Gets an ambient light from all the space. <br>
    #  False: Gets an ambient light only in the upper half space.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    MirroredExtent = property(fget = __GetMirroredExtent, fset = __SetMirroredExtent)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the spectrum type.
    # @details
    #  The values are:<br>
    #  0: Blackbody, then in the Temperature property, set the blackbody temperature of the source spectrum in Kdeg. <br>
    #  1: Library, then in the File property, browse a .spectrum file.
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    Spectrum = property(fget = __GetSpectrum, fset = __SetSpectrum)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or set the spectrum file path.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType property must be 1.<br>
    #  
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is an empty string.
    SpectrumFilePath = property(fget = __GetSpectrumFilePath, fset = __SetSpectrumFilePath)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the property to enable the Sun.
    # @details
    #  True : Uses the Sun.<br>
    #  False : Does not use the Sun.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    #  
    #  The default value is False.
    Sun = property(fget = __GetSun, fset = __SetSun)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the Sun direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseSun property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  The Sun direction property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    SunDirection = property(fget = __GetSunDirection, fset = __SetSunDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reverse Sun direction.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The UseSun property must be True.<br>
    #  
    #  True: Reverses the Sun direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the Sun directio.n<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    SunDirectionReverse = property(fget = __GetSunDirectionReverse, fset = __SetSunDirectionReverse)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the temperature.
    # @details
    #  <b>Prerequisite</b>: The SpectrumType property must be 0.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: String.<br>
    #  <b>Range</b>: The value must be superior to 0.0.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 8000.0 Kelvin.
    Temperature = property(fget = __GetTemperature, fset = __SetTemperature)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the zenith direction.
    # @details
    #  The zenith direction property takes a feature tag and returns a feature tag.<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Integer.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is 0.
    ZenithDirection = property(fget = __GetZenithDirection, fset = __SetZenithDirection)
    ##
    # @brief Gets or sets the reverse zenith direction.
    # @details
    #  True: Reverses the zenith direction.<br>
    #  False: Does not reverse the zenith direction<br>
    # 
    #  <b>Value type</b>: Boolean.<br>
    # 
    #  The default value is False.
    ZenithDirectionReversed = property(fget = __GetZenithDirectionReversed, fset = __SetZenithDirectionReversed)

    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_SourceAmbientUniformBuilder
    __del__ = lambda self: None

class PartCollection(_object):
    """@brief Represents the collection of all parts in a Speos For NX session."""

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, PartCollection, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, PartCollection, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_PartCollection
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def Load(self):
        """@brief Loads all open parts in the session."""
        return _SpeosNX.PartCollection_Load(self)


    def FindFromName(self, name):
        """
        @brief Finds the part with the given name.

         <b>Prerequisite</b>: The part must have been loaded in this session.
        @param[in] name : String.
        @return The part with the given name.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.PartCollection_FindFromName(self, name)


    def FindFromTag(self, tag):
        """
        @brief Finds the part with the given Tag.
        @param[in] tag : Integer. The Part Tag.
        @return The part with the given Tag.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.PartCollection_FindFromTag(self, tag)


    def __GetWork(self):
        return _SpeosNX.PartCollection___GetWork(self)

    def __GetDisplay(self):
        return _SpeosNX.PartCollection___GetDisplay(self)

    ##
    # @brief Returns the currently active display part of the session. 
    # @return The currently active display part.
    Display = property(fget = __GetDisplay)
    ##
    # @brief Returns the current work part of the session.
    # @return The current work part.
    Work = property(fget = __GetWork)

PartCollection_swigregister = _SpeosNX.PartCollection_swigregister
PartCollection_swigregister(PartCollection)

class Session(_object):
    """@brief Represents the Speos For NX session."""

    __swig_setmethods__ = {}
    __setattr__ = lambda self, name, value: _swig_setattr(self, Session, name, value)
    __swig_getmethods__ = {}
    __getattr__ = lambda self, name: _swig_getattr(self, Session, name)

    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise AttributeError("No constructor defined")
    __repr__ = _swig_repr
    __swig_destroy__ = _SpeosNX.delete_Session
    __del__ = lambda self: None

    def GetSession():
        """
        @brief Gets the unique instance of the Speos For NX session.
        @details 
         Returns the singleton for @link Session @endlink.
        @return The Speos For NX session.
        """
        return _SpeosNX.Session_GetSession()

    GetSession = staticmethod(GetSession)

    def __GetNXSessionTag(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Session___GetNXSessionTag(self)

    def __GetParts(self):
        return _SpeosNX.Session___GetParts(self)

    ##
    # @brief Gets the NX Session Tag.
    # @details 
    #  Returns the Tag for the NX Session.
    # @return The Tag as an integer.
    NXSessionTag = property(fget = __GetNXSessionTag)
    ##
    # @brief Gets the part collection.
    # @details 
    #  Returns the @link PartCollection @endlink belonging to this session.
    # @return The @link PartCollection @endlink.
    Parts = property(fget = __GetParts)

Session_swigregister = _SpeosNX.Session_swigregister
Session_swigregister(Session)

def Session_GetSession():
    """
    @brief Gets the unique instance of the Speos For NX session.
    @details 
     Returns the singleton for @link Session @endlink.
    @return The Speos For NX session.
    """
    return _SpeosNX.Session_GetSession()
